    <!-- Service Worker Unregistration - ONE-TIME CHECK -->
    <script>
    // Only run once per session to clear old service workers
    if ('serviceWorker' in navigator && !sessionStorage.getItem('sw_cleared_v2')) {
        navigator.serviceWorker.getRegistrations().then(function(registrations) {
            if (registrations.length > 0) {
                registrations.forEach(registration => registration.unregister());
                if ('caches' in window) {
                    caches.keys().then(names => names.forEach(name => caches.delete(name)));
                }
                sessionStorage.setItem('sw_cleared_v2', '1');
                if (window.nirivNotify) {
                    window.nirivNotify.log('Service workers cleared', 'info');
                }
            } else {
                sessionStorage.setItem('sw_cleared_v2', '1');
            }
        });
    }
    </script>

                            <script>
                                // Initialize notification system when DOM is ready
                                function setupNotificationDropdown() {
                                    // Initialize the notification system only if not already initialized
                                    if (typeof NirivNotificationSystem !== 'undefined' && !window.nirivNotificationSystem) {
                                        window.nirivNotificationSystem = new NirivNotificationSystem();
                                    }
                                    
                                    // Keep existing tab switching functionality
                                    const notificationButton = document.getElementById('notification-button');
                                    const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notification-dropdown');
                                    const newPostsTab = document.getElementById('new-posts-tab');
                                    const notificationsTab = document.getElementById('notifications-tab');
                                    const newPostsContent = document.getElementById('new-posts-content');
                                    const notificationsContent = document.getElementById('notifications-content');

                                    if (!notificationButton) {
                                        // Button not found yet, try again after a short delay
                                        setTimeout(setupNotificationDropdown, 100);
                                        return;
                                    }

                                    // Toggle dropdown with smooth animation
                                    // Let notification system handle it if available, otherwise handle manually
                                    notificationButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                        e.stopPropagation();
                                        
                                        // Close other dropdowns first
                                        const userDropdown = document.getElementById('user-dropdown');
                                        const chatTeaserDropdown = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-dropdown');
                                        if (userDropdown && !userDropdown.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                                            closeDropdown(userDropdown);
                                        }
                                        if (chatTeaserDropdown && !chatTeaserDropdown.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                                            closeDropdown(chatTeaserDropdown);
                                        }
                                        
                                        // If notification system is initialized, use it to toggle
                                        if (window.nirivNotificationSystem && window.nirivNotificationSystem.isInitialized) {
                                            // Use the notification system's toggle method
                                            // It will handle the dropdown state and loading
                                            window.nirivNotificationSystem.toggleDropdown();
                                        } else {
                                            // Fallback: handle manually if notification system not available
                                            if (notificationDropdown && notificationDropdown.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                                                openDropdown(notificationDropdown);
                                            } else if (notificationDropdown) {
                                                closeDropdown(notificationDropdown);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                    
                                    // Setup tab switching after button is ready
                                    setupTabSwitching();
                                }
                                
                                // Function to refresh new posts content
                                function refreshNewPostsContent() {
                                    // This function is handled by the server-side PHP code
                                    // The content is regenerated each time the tab is clicked
                                    return true;
                                }
                                
                                function setupTabSwitching() {
                                    const newPostsTab = document.getElementById('new-posts-tab');
                                    const notificationsTab = document.getElementById('notifications-tab');
                                    const newPostsContent = document.getElementById('new-posts-content');
                                    const notificationsContent = document.getElementById('notifications-content');
                                    
                                    if (!newPostsTab || !notificationsTab) return;
                                
                                    // Switch to new posts tab
                                    newPostsTab.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                        e.stopPropagation();
                                        
                                        newPostsTab.classList.remove('text-gray-500', 'hover:text-gray-700');
                                        newPostsTab.classList.add('text-blue-600', 'border-b-2', 'border-blue-600');

                                        notificationsTab.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'border-b-2', 'border-blue-600');
                                        notificationsTab.classList.add('text-gray-500', 'hover:text-gray-700');

                                        if (newPostsContent) {
                                            newPostsContent.classList.remove('hidden');
                                            newPostsContent.style.display = 'flex';
                                        }
                                        if (notificationsContent) {
                                            notificationsContent.classList.add('hidden');
                                            notificationsContent.style.display = 'none';
                                        }
                                        
                                        // Refresh new posts content when tab is clicked
                                        refreshNewPostsContent();
                                    });

                                    // Switch to notifications tab
                                    notificationsTab.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                        e.stopPropagation();
                                        
                                        notificationsTab.classList.remove('text-gray-500', 'hover:text-gray-700');
                                        notificationsTab.classList.add('text-blue-600', 'border-b-2', 'border-blue-600');

                                        newPostsTab.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'border-b-2', 'border-blue-600');
                                        newPostsTab.classList.add('text-gray-500', 'hover:text-gray-700');

                                        if (notificationsContent) {
                                            notificationsContent.classList.remove('hidden');
                                            notificationsContent.style.display = 'flex';
                                        }
                                        if (newPostsContent) {
                                            newPostsContent.classList.add('hidden');
                                            newPostsContent.style.display = 'none';
                                        }
                                        
                                        // Load notifications when tab is clicked (force refresh)
                                        // But only if not already loading (prevents infinite loop)
                                        if (window.nirivNotificationSystem && !window.nirivNotificationSystem.isLoadingNotifications) {
                                            window.nirivNotificationSystem.loadNotifications(true);
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                                
                                // Initialize when DOM is ready
                                if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                                    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                                        // Small delay to ensure all scripts are loaded
                                        setTimeout(setupNotificationDropdown, 100);
                                    });
                                } else {
                                    // DOM already loaded
                                    // Small delay to ensure all scripts are loaded
                                    setTimeout(setupNotificationDropdown, 100);
                                }
                            </script>

    <script>
        // Helper functions for smooth dropdown animations (global scope)
        function openDropdown(dropdown) {
            dropdown.classList.remove('hidden');
            // Force reflow
            dropdown.offsetHeight;
            dropdown.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'scale-95', 'translate-y-1', 'pointer-events-none');
            dropdown.classList.add('opacity-100', 'scale-100', 'translate-y-0', 'pointer-events-auto');
        }

        function closeDropdown(dropdown) {
            dropdown.classList.remove('opacity-100', 'scale-100', 'translate-y-0', 'pointer-events-auto');
            dropdown.classList.add('opacity-0', 'scale-95', 'translate-y-1', 'pointer-events-none');
            setTimeout(() => {
                dropdown.classList.add('hidden');
            }, 200);
        }

        // Chat Teaser Dropdown Functionality
        const chatTeaserButton = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-button');
        const chatTeaserDropdown = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-dropdown');
        const chatTeaserInput = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-input');
        const chatTeaserSend = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-send');
        const charCount = document.getElementById('char-count');

        if (chatTeaserButton && chatTeaserDropdown) {
            // Toggle chat teaser dropdown
            chatTeaserButton.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                
                // Close other dropdowns
                const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notification-dropdown');
                const userDropdown = document.getElementById('user-dropdown');
                if (notificationDropdown && !notificationDropdown.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                    closeDropdown(notificationDropdown);
                }
                if (userDropdown && !userDropdown.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                    closeDropdown(userDropdown);
                }

                // Toggle chat teaser dropdown
                if (chatTeaserDropdown.classList.contains('hidden')) {
                    openDropdown(chatTeaserDropdown);
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        if (chatTeaserInput) {
                            chatTeaserInput.focus();
                        }
                    }, 100);
                } else {
                    closeDropdown(chatTeaserDropdown);
                }
            });

            // Prevent dropdown from closing when clicking inside it
            chatTeaserDropdown.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
            });

            // Character count
            if (chatTeaserInput && charCount) {
                chatTeaserInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
                    const length = this.value.length;
                    charCount.textContent = length + '/200';
                    
                    // Enable/disable send button
                    if (chatTeaserSend) {
                        chatTeaserSend.disabled = length === 0;
                    }
                });
            }

            // Send to Baje
            if (chatTeaserSend) {
                chatTeaserSend.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    const message = chatTeaserInput.value.trim();
                    if (message) {
                        // Store message in localStorage for the chat page
                        localStorage.setItem('baje_teaser_message', message);
                        
                        // Redirect to Baje chat page
                        window.location.href = '/baje';
                    }
                });
            }

            // Enter key to send
            if (chatTeaserInput) {
                chatTeaserInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        if (chatTeaserSend && !chatTeaserSend.disabled) {
                            chatTeaserSend.click();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        // Global click handler to close all dropdowns when clicking outside
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            const notificationDropdown = document.getElementById('notification-dropdown');
            const userDropdown = document.getElementById('user-dropdown');
            const chatTeaserDropdown = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-dropdown');
            const notificationButton = document.getElementById('notification-button');
            const userButton = document.getElementById('user-menu-button');
            const chatTeaserButton = document.getElementById('chat-teaser-button');

            // Close notification dropdown if clicking outside
            if (notificationDropdown && !notificationDropdown.classList.contains('hidden') &&
                (!notificationButton || !notificationButton.contains(e.target))) {
                closeDropdown(notificationDropdown);
            }

            // Close user dropdown if clicking outside
            if (userDropdown && !userDropdown.classList.contains('hidden') &&
                (!userButton || !userButton.contains(e.target)) &&
                (!userDropdown || !userDropdown.contains(e.target))) {
                closeDropdown(userDropdown);
            }

            // Close chat teaser dropdown if clicking outside (but not inside the dropdown)
            if (chatTeaserDropdown && !chatTeaserDropdown.classList.contains('hidden') &&
                (!chatTeaserButton || !chatTeaserButton.contains(e.target)) &&
                (!chatTeaserDropdown || !chatTeaserDropdown.contains(e.target))) {
                closeDropdown(chatTeaserDropdown);
            }
        });
    </script>


    <script>
    // Lucide icons initialization
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
            lucide.createIcons();
        }
        
        // Mobile menu scroll visibility control
        const mobileMenu = document.getElementById('sticky-mobile-menu');
        if (mobileMenu) {
            let isScrolling = false;
            let scrollTimeout;
            
            function handleScroll() {
                if (!isScrolling) {
                    window.requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                        const scrollY = window.scrollY || window.pageYOffset;
                        
                        if (scrollY > 250) {
                            mobileMenu.style.display = 'none';
                        } else {
                            mobileMenu.style.display = 'block';
                        }
                        
                        isScrolling = false;
                    });
                }
                isScrolling = true;
            }
            
            // Throttled scroll listener for better performance
            let ticking = false;
            function throttledScroll() {
                if (!ticking) {
                    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                        handleScroll();
                        ticking = false;
                    });
                    ticking = true;
                }
            }
            
            window.addEventListener('scroll', throttledScroll, { passive: true });
            
            // Initial check
            handleScroll();
        }
    });
    
    // Check for open_sidebar parameter and open sidebar
    // Use multiple methods to ensure it works after sidebar initialization
    function openSidebarIfRequested() {
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        if (urlParams.get('open_sidebar') === '1') {
            const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
            const sidebarOverlay = document.getElementById('sidebar-overlay');
            const menuBtn = document.getElementById('menu-toggle-btn');
            
            if (sidebar && sidebarOverlay) {
                // Directly open sidebar by manipulating classes (bypassing any close handlers)
                sidebar.classList.remove('-translate-x-full', 'opacity-0');
                sidebar.classList.add('opacity-100');
                sidebar.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
                sidebar.removeAttribute('inert');
                sidebarOverlay.classList.remove('opacity-0', 'invisible', 'hidden');
                sidebarOverlay.classList.add('opacity-100', 'visible');
                document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                return true;
            } else if (menuBtn) {
                // Fallback: click the button
                menuBtn.click();
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
    
    // Try after pageshow event (which closes sidebar) - use longer delay
    window.addEventListener('pageshow', function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            if (openSidebarIfRequested()) {
                // Keep trying to ensure it stays open
                setTimeout(openSidebarIfRequested, 200);
                setTimeout(openSidebarIfRequested, 500);
            }
        }, 400);
    });
    
    // Also try on DOMContentLoaded and load
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        setTimeout(openSidebarIfRequested, 600);
        setTimeout(openSidebarIfRequested, 1200);
    });
    
    window.addEventListener('load', function() {
        setTimeout(openSidebarIfRequested, 800);
    });
    </script>

    <main>

<!-- Autocomplete Functionality for 404 Search Form -->
<script>
(function() {
    // Prevent double autosuggest - mark that autocomplete is already initialized
    if (window.nirivAutocompleteInitialized404) return;
    window.nirivAutocompleteInitialized404 = true;
    
    const searchInput = document.getElementById('main-search-input-404');
    const autocompleteResults = document.getElementById('autocomplete-results-404');
    let currentSelectedIndex = -1;
    let autocompleteItems = [];
    let debounceTimer;

    if (!searchInput || !autocompleteResults) return;

    // Show autocomplete dropdown with Google suggestions
    function showAutocomplete(query) {
        if (query.length < 1) {
            hideAutocomplete();
            return;
        }

        // Debounce API calls
        clearTimeout(debounceTimer);
        debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
            loadGoogleAutocomplete(query);
        }, 150);
    }

    // Load Google autocomplete suggestions
    function loadGoogleAutocomplete(query) {
        // Clear any previous callback
        if (window.handle404Autocomplete) {
            delete window.handle404Autocomplete;
        }
        
        window.handle404Autocomplete = (data) => {
            const suggestions = data && data[1] ? data[1] : [];
            
            if (!suggestions || suggestions.length === 0) {
                hideAutocomplete();
                return;
            }

            autocompleteResults.innerHTML = '';
            autocompleteItems = [];

            suggestions.slice(0, 8).forEach((item, index) => {
                if (!item || typeof item !== 'string') return;
                
                const div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'px-4 py-3 cursor-pointer border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 hover:bg-gray-50 transition-colors flex items-center';
                div.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff';
                div.style.color = '#374151';
                div.style.fontWeight = 'normal';
                div.innerHTML = `<i data-lucide="search" class="w-4 h-4 mr-3 text-gray-400"></i><span>${item}</span>`;
                div.dataset.index = index;
                div.setAttribute('id', 'autocomplete-option-404-' + index);
                div.setAttribute('role', 'option');
                div.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'false');
                
                div.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
                    currentSelectedIndex = parseInt(this.dataset.index);
                    updateSelectedItem();
                });
                
                div.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    const textSpan = this.querySelector('span');
                    const itemText = textSpan ? textSpan.textContent : this.textContent;
                    selectItem(itemText);
                });

                autocompleteResults.appendChild(div);
                autocompleteItems.push(div);
            });

            if (autocompleteItems.length > 0) {
                autocompleteResults.classList.remove('hidden');
                searchInput.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
                currentSelectedIndex = -1;
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                    lucide.createIcons();
                }
            } else {
                hideAutocomplete();
            }

            delete window.handle404Autocomplete;
        };

        // Load Google autocomplete script
        const script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = `https://suggestqueries.google.com/complete/search?client=chrome&q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&callback=handle404Autocomplete`;
        script.onerror = function() {
            hideAutocomplete();
            delete window.handle404Autocomplete;
        };
        document.head.appendChild(script);
        script.remove();
    }

    // Hide autocomplete dropdown
    function hideAutocomplete() {
        autocompleteResults.classList.add('hidden');
        searchInput.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        currentSelectedIndex = -1;
    }

    // Select an item
    function selectItem(item) {
        searchInput.value = item;
        hideAutocomplete();
        searchInput.closest('form').submit();
    }

    // Update selected item styling
    function updateSelectedItem() {
        autocompleteItems.forEach((item, index) => {
            if (index === currentSelectedIndex) {
                item.style.backgroundColor = '#eff6ff';
                const textSpan = item.querySelector('span');
                if (textSpan) {
                    textSpan.style.color = '#1847ea';
                    textSpan.style.fontWeight = '500';
                }
                const icon = item.querySelector('i[data-lucide="search"]');
                if (icon) {
                    icon.style.color = '#1847ea';
                }
                item.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'true');
                searchInput.setAttribute('aria-activedescendant', item.id);
            } else {
                item.style.backgroundColor = '#ffffff';
                const textSpan = item.querySelector('span');
                if (textSpan) {
                    textSpan.style.color = '#374151';
                    textSpan.style.fontWeight = 'normal';
                }
                const icon = item.querySelector('i[data-lucide="search"]');
                if (icon) {
                    icon.style.color = '#9ca3af';
                }
                item.setAttribute('aria-selected', 'false');
            }
        });
        
        if (currentSelectedIndex >= 0 && autocompleteItems[currentSelectedIndex]) {
            autocompleteItems[currentSelectedIndex].scrollIntoView({
                block: 'nearest',
                behavior: 'smooth'
            });
        } else {
            searchInput.removeAttribute('aria-activedescendant');
        }
    }

    // Handle input events
    searchInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
        const query = this.value;
        showAutocomplete(query);
    });

    // Handle keyboard navigation
    searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (autocompleteResults.classList.contains('hidden') || autocompleteItems.length === 0) {
            return;
        }

        switch(e.key) {
            case 'ArrowDown':
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                if (currentSelectedIndex < autocompleteItems.length - 1) {
                    currentSelectedIndex++;
                } else {
                    currentSelectedIndex = 0;
                }
                updateSelectedItem();
                break;
            
            case 'ArrowUp':
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                if (currentSelectedIndex > 0) {
                    currentSelectedIndex--;
                } else {
                    currentSelectedIndex = autocompleteItems.length - 1;
                }
                updateSelectedItem();
                break;
            
            case 'Enter':
                if (currentSelectedIndex >= 0 && autocompleteItems[currentSelectedIndex]) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    const selectedItem = autocompleteItems[currentSelectedIndex];
                    const textSpan = selectedItem.querySelector('span');
                    const itemText = textSpan ? textSpan.textContent : selectedItem.textContent;
                    selectItem(itemText);
                }
                break;
            
            case 'Escape':
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                hideAutocomplete();
                break;
        }
    }, true);

    // Hide autocomplete when clicking outside
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (!searchInput.contains(e.target) && !autocompleteResults.contains(e.target)) {
            hideAutocomplete();
        }
    });

    // Hide autocomplete on blur
    searchInput.addEventListener('blur', function() {
        setTimeout(() => {
            if (!autocompleteResults.matches(':hover')) {
                hideAutocomplete();
            }
        }, 200);
    });
})();
</script>

<script>
    // Initialize Lucide icons
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
            lucide.createIcons();
        }
    });
</script>

<!-- Referral Code Cookie Tracking -->
<script>
(function() {
    'use strict';
    
    // Function to set cookie
    function setCookie(name, value, days) {
        var expires = '';
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();
        }
        var secure = window.location.protocol === 'https:' ? '; Secure' : '';
        document.cookie = name + '=' + encodeURIComponent(value) + expires + '; path=/' + secure + '; SameSite=Lax';
    }
    
    // Function to get cookie
    function getCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + '=';
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) === ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0) return decodeURIComponent(c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length));
        }
        return null;
    }
    
    // Check for referral code in URL
    function trackReferralCode() {
        var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        var refCode = urlParams.get('ref');
        
        if (refCode && refCode.trim() !== '') {
            // Set cookie for 7 days
            setCookie('niriv_referral_code', refCode.trim(), 7);
        }
    }
    
    // Run on page load
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', trackReferralCode);
    } else {
        trackReferralCode();
    }
})();
</script>

        <script>
    (function() {
        /**
         * Add rel="ugc" to all links pointing to cafe posts
         */
        function addUgcRelToCafeLinks() {
            // Find all links that point to cafe posts
            const links = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/cafe/post/"]');
            links.forEach(function(link) {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                if (href && href.includes('/cafe/post/')) {
                    // Check if rel="ugc" already exists
                    const existingRel = link.getAttribute('rel');
                    if (existingRel) {
                        // If rel exists but doesn't contain "ugc", add it
                        if (!existingRel.includes('ugc')) {
                            link.setAttribute('rel', existingRel + ' ugc');
                        }
                    } else {
                        // No rel attribute, add it
                        link.setAttribute('rel', 'ugc');
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Run on page load
        if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', addUgcRelToCafeLinks);
        } else {
            addUgcRelToCafeLinks();
        }
        
        // Watch for dynamically added content (AJAX, infinite scroll, etc.)
        const observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
            let shouldCheck = false;
            mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
                if (mutation.addedNodes.length > 0) {
                    shouldCheck = true;
                }
            });
            if (shouldCheck) {
                addUgcRelToCafeLinks();
            }
        });
        
        // Start observing the document body for changes
        if (document.body) {
            observer.observe(document.body, {
                childList: true,
                subtree: true
            });
        } else {
            // If body doesn't exist yet, wait for it
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                if (document.body) {
                    observer.observe(document.body, {
                        childList: true,
                        subtree: true
                    });
                }
            });
        }
    })();
    </script>
