        <script>
        (function() {
            'use strict';
            
            async function toggleFollowForLikers(userId, button) {
                if (!button) return;
                
                // Check if user is logged in
                let isLoggedIn = false;
                if (typeof nirivAjax !== 'undefined') {
                    isLoggedIn = nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in === '1' ||
                                 nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in === 1 ||
                                 nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in === true ||
                                 nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in ||
                                 nirivAjax.logged_in === '1' ||
                                 nirivAjax.logged_in === 1 ||
                                 nirivAjax.logged_in === true ||
                                 nirivAjax.logged_in ||
                                 nirivAjax.loggedIn === '1' ||
                                 nirivAjax.loggedIn === 1 ||
                                 nirivAjax.loggedIn === true ||
                                 nirivAjax.loggedIn;
                } else if (typeof nirivFollow !== 'undefined') {
                    isLoggedIn = nirivFollow.logged_in === '1' ||
                                 nirivFollow.logged_in === 1 ||
                                 nirivFollow.logged_in === true ||
                                 nirivFollow.logged_in;
                }
                
                if (!isLoggedIn) {
                    // Show message and redirect to login
                    if (window.nirivToast) {
                        window.nirivToast.show('Please log in to follow', 'info', 2000);
                    }
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        window.location.href = '/nid';
                    }, 500);
                    return;
                }
                
                // Ensure userId is a number
                const numericUserId = parseInt(userId, 10);
                if (!numericUserId || isNaN(numericUserId)) {
                    if (window.nirivToast) {
                        window.nirivToast.show('Invalid user ID', 'error', 2000);
                    }
                    return;
                }
                
                // Try to use global follow system if available
                if (typeof FollowSystem !== 'undefined' && FollowSystem.state && FollowSystem.state.initialized && typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
                    try {
                        const $button = jQuery(button);
                        const isFollowing = button.dataset.following === 'true';
                        // Ensure button has required data attributes for follow system
                        $button.data('id', numericUserId);
                        $button.data('type', 'user');
                        $button.data('following', isFollowing);
                        FollowSystem.toggleFollow($button, numericUserId, 'user', isFollowing);
                        return;
                    } catch (e) {
                        // Fall through to direct AJAX
                    }
                }
                
                const isFollowing = button.dataset.following === 'true';
                button.disabled = true;
                button.style.opacity = '0.6';
                
                // Get nonce from multiple possible sources
                let nonce = '';
                let ajaxUrl = '/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';
                
                if (typeof nirivAjax !== 'undefined') {
                    nonce = nirivAjax.nonce || '';
                    ajaxUrl = nirivAjax.ajaxurl || ajaxUrl;
                } else if (typeof nirivFollow !== 'undefined') {
                    nonce = nirivFollow.nonce || '';
                    ajaxUrl = nirivFollow.ajaxurl || ajaxUrl;
                } else if (typeof niriv_ajax !== 'undefined') {
                    nonce = niriv_ajax.nonce || '';
                    ajaxUrl = niriv_ajax.ajaxurl || ajaxUrl;
                }
                
                // If still no nonce, try to get from meta tag
                if (!nonce) {
                    const metaNonce = document.querySelector('meta[name="niriv-ajax-nonce"]');
                    if (metaNonce) {
                        nonce = metaNonce.getAttribute('content') || '';
                    }
                }
                
                if (!nonce) {
                    if (window.nirivToast) {
                        window.nirivToast.show('Security token missing. Please refresh the page.', 'error', 2000);
                    }
                    button.disabled = false;
                    button.style.opacity = '1';
                    return;
                }

                const fd = new FormData();
                fd.append('action', 'toggle_follow');
                fd.append('nonce', nonce);
                fd.append('_ajax_nonce', nonce); // Also send as _ajax_nonce for compatibility
                fd.append('object_id', String(numericUserId)); // Use the numericUserId from earlier
                fd.append('object_type', 'user');

                try {
                    const res = await fetch(ajaxUrl, { method:'POST', body: fd });
                    
                    if (!res.ok) {
                        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${res.status}`);
                    }
                    
                    const data = await res.json();
                    
                    if(data?.success){
                        const newState = !isFollowing;
                        button.dataset.following = newState ? 'true' : 'false';
                        button.textContent = newState ? 'Following' : 'Follow';
                        button.classList.toggle('following', newState);
                        
                        // Show success message
                        if (window.nirivToast) {
                            window.nirivToast.show(data?.data?.message || 'Success', 'success', 2000);
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (window.nirivToast) {
                            window.nirivToast.show(data?.data?.message || 'An error occurred', 'error', 2000);
                        }
                    }
                } catch (error) {
                    if (window.nirivToast) {
                        window.nirivToast.show('An error occurred. Please try again.', 'error', 2000);
                    }
                } finally {
                    button.disabled = false;
                    button.style.opacity = '1';
                }
            }
            
            const NirivLikeSystem = {
                ajaxUrl: 'https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
                nonce: '0d3d305449',
                
                init: function() {
                    this.attachEventListeners();
                    this.observeDOMChanges();
                },
                
                observeDOMChanges: function() {
                    // Re-attach event listeners when new content is added to the DOM
                    const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
                        // Silent observation - event delegation handles new buttons automatically
                    });
                    
                    // Observe the entire document for changes
                    observer.observe(document.body, {
                        childList: true,
                        subtree: true
                    });
                },
                
                initDragToClose: function() {
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-liked-users-modal');
                    const modalContent = modal?.querySelector('.niriv-liked-users-modal-content');
                    const dragHandle = modalContent?.querySelector('.niriv-modal-drag-handle');
                    if (!modalContent || !dragHandle) return;

                    let startY = 0;
                    let currentY = 0;
                    let isDragging = false;
                    let startTime = 0;

                    const handleStart = (e) => {
                        const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
                        startY = touch.clientY;
                        currentY = startY;
                        isDragging = true;
                        startTime = Date.now();
                        modalContent.style.transition = 'none';
                        e.preventDefault();
                    };

                    const handleMove = (e) => {
                        if (!isDragging) return;
                        const touch = e.touches ? e.touches[0] : e;
                        currentY = touch.clientY;
                        const deltaY = currentY - startY;
                        
                        if (deltaY > 0) {
                            modalContent.style.transform = `translateY(${deltaY}px)`;
                            const opacity = Math.max(0, 1 - (deltaY / 300));
                            modalContent.style.opacity = opacity;
                        }
                        e.preventDefault();
                    };

                    const handleEnd = () => {
                        if (!isDragging) return;
                        isDragging = false;
                        modalContent.style.transition = '';
                        
                        const deltaY = currentY - startY;
                        const deltaTime = Date.now() - startTime;
                        const velocity = deltaY / deltaTime;
                        
                        // Close if dragged more than 100px or with sufficient velocity
                        if (deltaY > 100 || velocity > 0.5) {
                            this.closeLikedUsersModal();
                        } else {
                            // Snap back
                            modalContent.style.transform = '';
                            modalContent.style.opacity = '';
                        }
                    };

                    dragHandle.addEventListener('mousedown', handleStart);
                    dragHandle.addEventListener('touchstart', handleStart, { passive: false });
                    
                    document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMove);
                    document.addEventListener('touchmove', handleMove, { passive: false });
                    
                    document.addEventListener('mouseup', handleEnd);
                    document.addEventListener('touchend', handleEnd);
                },
                
                attachEventListeners: function() {
                    // Initialize drag to close
                    this.initDragToClose();
                    
                    // Like button clicks
                    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                        const likeBtn = e.target.closest('.niriv-like-btn');
                        if (likeBtn) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            this.toggleLike(likeBtn);
                        }
                        
                        // Like count clicks (show modal)
                        const likeCount = e.target.closest('.niriv-like-count.clickable');
                        if (likeCount) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            const postId = likeCount.dataset.postId;
                            this.showLikedUsers(postId);
                        }
                    });
                    
                    // Click outside to close
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-liked-users-modal');
                    if (modal) {
                        modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                            if (e.target === modal) {
                                this.closeLikedUsersModal();
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // Escape key to close
                    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                        if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                            this.closeLikedUsersModal();
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                toggleLike: function(button) {
                    const postId = button.dataset.postId;
                    const isLiked = button.dataset.liked === '1';
                    const actionType = isLiked ? 'unlike' : 'like';
                    
                    // Optimistic UI update
                    button.classList.toggle('liked');
                    button.classList.add('animating');
                    button.dataset.liked = isLiked ? '0' : '1';
                    
                    setTimeout(() => button.classList.remove('animating'), 400);
                    
                    // Update all like buttons for this post
                    const allButtons = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-like-btn[data-post-id="${postId}"]`);
                    allButtons.forEach(btn => {
                        if (btn !== button) {
                            btn.classList.toggle('liked');
                            btn.dataset.liked = isLiked ? '0' : '1';
                        }
                    });
                    
                    // AJAX call
                    fetch(this.ajaxUrl, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                        },
                        body: new URLSearchParams({
                            action: 'niriv_toggle_like',
                            nonce: this.nonce,
                            post_id: postId,
                            action_type: actionType
                        })
                    })
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        if (data.success) {
                            // Update counts
                            this.updateLikeCounts(postId, data.data.count);
                            
                            // Show toast
                            if (window.nirivToast) {
                                window.nirivToast.show(data.data.message, 'success', 2000);
                            }
                        } else {
                            // Revert on error
                            button.classList.toggle('liked');
                            button.dataset.liked = isLiked ? '1' : '0';
                            
                            if (window.nirivToast) {
                                window.nirivToast.show('Error: ' + data.data.message, 'error', 3000);
                            }
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log('Like error: ' + (error?.message || error), 'error');
                        }
                        // Revert on error
                        button.classList.toggle('liked');
                        button.dataset.liked = isLiked ? '1' : '0';
                        
                        if (window.nirivToast) {
                            window.nirivToast.show('Network error', 'error', 3000);
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                updateLikeCounts: function(postId, count) {
                    const counters = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-like-count[data-post-id="${postId}"]`);
                    counters.forEach(counter => {
                        // Hide counter if count is 0, show if count > 0
                        if (count === 0) {
                            counter.style.display = 'none';
                        } else {
                            counter.style.display = '';
                            counter.textContent = new Intl.NumberFormat().format(count);
                            
                            // Toggle clickable class based on count
                            if (count > 0 && !counter.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                                counter.classList.add('clickable');
                            } else if (count === 0 && counter.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                                counter.classList.remove('clickable');
                            }
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                showLikedUsers: function(postId) {
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-liked-users-modal');
                    const modalContent = modal?.querySelector('.niriv-liked-users-modal-content');
                    const body = document.getElementById('niriv-liked-users-body');
                    
                    if (!modal || !body) return;
                    
                    // Reset any inline styles from previous drag interactions
                    if(modalContent) {
                        modalContent.style.transform = '';
                        modalContent.style.opacity = '';
                        modalContent.style.transition = '';
                    }
                    
                    // Lock body scroll
                    const scrollY = window.scrollY;
                    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                    document.body.style.position = 'fixed';
                    document.body.style.width = '100%';
                    document.body.style.top = `-${scrollY}px`;
                    
                    // Show modal with loading state
                    modal.classList.add('active');
                    body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-liked-users-loading"><div class="niriv-spinner"></div></div>';
                    
                    // Fetch liked users
                    fetch(this.ajaxUrl, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                        },
                        body: new URLSearchParams({
                            action: 'niriv_get_liked_users',
                            nonce: this.nonce,
                            post_id: postId
                        })
                    })
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        if (data.success) {
                            this.updateModalHeader(data.data);
                            this.renderLikedUsers(data.data.users);
                        } else {
                            body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-liked-users-empty">Error loading users</div>';
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log('Error fetching liked users: ' + (error?.message || error), 'error');
                        }
                        body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-liked-users-empty">Error loading users</div>';
                    });
                },
                
                updateModalHeader: function(data) {
                    const titleElement = document.querySelector('.niriv-liked-users-modal-title');
                    const subtitleElement = document.querySelector('.niriv-liked-users-modal-subtitle');
                    
                    if (!titleElement || !subtitleElement) return;
                    
                    const totalCount = data.total_count || 0;
                    const loggedInCount = data.logged_in_count || 0;
                    const guestCount = data.guest_count || 0;
                    
                    // Update title with total count
                    if (totalCount > 0) {
                        titleElement.textContent = `Liked by ${totalCount.toLocaleString()}`;
                    } else {
                        titleElement.textContent = 'Liked by';
                    }
                    
                    // Update subtitle with breakdown
                    const parts = [];
                    if (loggedInCount > 0) {
                        parts.push(`${loggedInCount.toLocaleString()} user${loggedInCount !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`);
                    }
                    if (guestCount > 0) {
                        parts.push(`${guestCount.toLocaleString()} visitor${guestCount !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`);
                    }
                    
                    if (parts.length > 0) {
                        subtitleElement.textContent = parts.join(' • ');
                    } else {
                        subtitleElement.textContent = 'Not liked by users yet';
                    }
                },
                
                renderLikedUsers: function(users) {
                    const body = document.getElementById('niriv-liked-users-body');
                    if (!body) return;
                    
                    if (!users || users.length === 0) {
                        body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-liked-users-empty">Not liked by users yet</div>';
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    // Check login status once - try multiple property names
                    let loggedIn = false;
                    let currentUserId = 0;
                    
                    if (typeof nirivAjax !== 'undefined') {
                        // Try different property names for logged in status (check is_user_logged_in first as it's the standard)
                        loggedIn = nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in === '1' ||
                                   nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in === 1 ||
                                   nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in === true ||
                                   nirivAjax.is_user_logged_in ||
                                   nirivAjax.logged_in === '1' ||
                                   nirivAjax.logged_in === 1 ||
                                   nirivAjax.logged_in === true ||
                                   nirivAjax.logged_in ||
                                   nirivAjax.loggedIn === '1' || 
                                   nirivAjax.loggedIn === 1 || 
                                   nirivAjax.loggedIn === true || 
                                   nirivAjax.loggedIn;
                        
                        // Try different property names for current user ID (check current_user_id first as it's the standard)
                        currentUserId = parseInt(nirivAjax.current_user_id ||
                                                nirivAjax.currentUserId || 
                                                nirivAjax.userId || 
                                                nirivAjax.user_id ||
                                                0);
                    }
                    
                    const html = `
                        <div class="niriv-liked-users-list">
                            ${users.map(user => {
                                const isFollowing = user.is_following || false;
                                const followBtnText = isFollowing ? 'Following' : 'Follow';
                                const followBtnClass = isFollowing ? 'following' : '';
                                const userId = parseInt(user.id || 0);
                                const shouldShowButton = loggedIn && userId !== currentUserId && userId > 0;
                                
                                return `
                                <div class="niriv-liked-user-item">
                                    <img src="${user.avatar || ''}" alt="${user.name || ''}" class="niriv-liked-user-avatar" onerror="this.src='${typeof nirivAjax !== 'undefined' ? (nirivAjax.defaultAvatar || '') : ''}'">
                                    <div class="niriv-liked-user-info">
                                        <a href="${user.profile_url || '#'}" class="niriv-liked-user-name">${user.name || 'Unknown'}</a>
                                        ${user.username ? `<span class="niriv-liked-user-username">(@${user.username})</span>` : ''}
                                    </div>
                                    ${shouldShowButton ? `
                                        <div class="niriv-liked-user-action">
                                            <button class="niriv-liked-user-follow-btn ${followBtnClass}" 
                                                    data-user-id="${user.id}" 
                                                    data-following="${isFollowing}">
                                                ${followBtnText}
                                            </button>
                                        </div>
                                    ` : ''}
                                </div>
                            `;
                            }).join('')}
                        </div>
                    `;
                    
                    body.innerHTML = html;
                    
                    // Attach follow button handlers
                    body.querySelectorAll('.niriv-liked-user-follow-btn').forEach(btn => {
                        btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            const userId = btn.dataset.userId || btn.getAttribute('data-user-id');
                            if (!userId) {
                                return;
                            }
                            toggleFollowForLikers(userId, btn);
                        });
                    });
                },
                
                closeLikedUsersModal: function() {
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-liked-users-modal');
                    const modalContent = modal?.querySelector('.niriv-liked-users-modal-content');
                    
                    // Reset any inline styles from dragging
                    if(modalContent) {
                        modalContent.style.transform = '';
                        modalContent.style.opacity = '';
                        modalContent.style.transition = '';
                    }
                    
                    if (modal) {
                        modal.classList.remove('active');
                        
                        // Restore body scroll
                        const scrollY = document.body.style.top;
                        document.body.style.overflow = '';
                        document.body.style.position = '';
                        document.body.style.width = '';
                        document.body.style.top = '';
                        
                        if (scrollY) {
                            window.scrollTo(0, parseInt(scrollY || '0') * -1);
                        }
                    }
                }
            };
            
            // Initialize on DOM ready
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => NirivLikeSystem.init());
            } else {
                NirivLikeSystem.init();
            }
            
            // Make it globally accessible
            window.NirivLikeSystem = NirivLikeSystem;
        })();
        </script>
                <!-- Voted Users Modal -->
        <div id="niriv-voted-users-modal" class="niriv-voted-users-modal">
            <div class="niriv-voted-users-modal-content">
                <div class="niriv-voted-users-modal-header">
                    <div class="niriv-voted-users-modal-header-content">
                        <h3 class="niriv-voted-users-modal-title" id="niriv-voted-users-modal-title">Voted by</h3>
                        <p class="niriv-voted-users-modal-subtitle" id="niriv-voted-users-modal-subtitle">Loading...</p>
                    </div>
                    <button class="niriv-voted-users-modal-close" id="niriv-close-voted-modal" aria-label="Close">
                        <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round">
                            <line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18"></line>
                            <line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18"></line>
                        </svg>
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div class="niriv-voted-users-modal-body" id="niriv-voted-users-body">
                    <div class="niriv-voted-users-loading">
                        <div class="niriv-vote-spinner"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <script>
        (function() {
            'use strict';
            
            const NirivVotingSystem = {
                ajaxUrl: 'https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
                nonce: '5d790d8100',
                
                init: function() {
                    this.attachEventListeners();
                    this.observeDOMChanges();
                },
                
                observeDOMChanges: function() {
                    // Re-attach event listeners when new content is added to the DOM
                    const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
                        // Silent observation - event delegation handles new buttons automatically
                    });
                    
                    // Observe the entire document for changes
                    observer.observe(document.body, {
                        childList: true,
                        subtree: true
                    });
                },
                
                attachEventListeners: function() {
                    // Vote button clicks
                    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                        const voteBtn = e.target.closest('.niriv-vote-btn');
                        if (voteBtn && !voteBtn.disabled && !voteBtn.classList.contains('processing')) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            this.toggleVote(voteBtn);
                        }
                        
                        // Vote count clicks (show modal)
                        const voteCount = e.target.closest('.niriv-vote-count.clickable');
                        if (voteCount) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            const objectId = voteCount.dataset.objectId;
                            const objectType = voteCount.dataset.objectType || 'post';
                            const voteType = voteCount.dataset.voteType;
                            this.showVotedUsers(objectId, objectType, voteType);
                        }
                    });
                    
                    // Close modal
                    const closeBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-close-voted-modal');
                    if (closeBtn) {
                        closeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.closeVotedUsersModal());
                    }
                    
                    // Click outside to close
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-modal');
                    if (modal) {
                        modal.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                            if (e.target === modal) {
                                this.closeVotedUsersModal();
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // Escape key to close
                    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                        if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                            this.closeVotedUsersModal();
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                toggleVote: function(button) {
                    // Prevent double-clicks
                    if (button.disabled || button.classList.contains('processing')) {
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    const objectId = button.dataset.objectId;
                    const objectType = button.dataset.objectType || 'post';
                    const voteType = button.dataset.voteType; // upvote or downvote
                    const isVoted = button.dataset.voted === '1';
                    
                    // Get all vote buttons for this object first
                    const allVoteBtns = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-btn[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    
                    // Disable all vote buttons for this object to prevent double-clicks
                    // Use setTimeout to ensure the click event has fully processed
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        allVoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                            btn.disabled = true;
                            btn.classList.add('processing');
                            btn.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
                        });
                    }, 0);
                    
                    // Get all vote buttons for this object
                    const allUpvoteBtns = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-upvote[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    const allDownvoteBtns = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-downvote[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    
                    // Check current state
                    const isUpvoted = allUpvoteBtns.length > 0 && allUpvoteBtns[0].dataset.voted === '1';
                    const isDownvoted = allDownvoteBtns.length > 0 && allDownvoteBtns[0].dataset.voted === '1';
                    
                    // Determine action: if clicking the same button that's already voted, remove it
                    // Otherwise, vote (server will handle removing opposite vote)
                    let actionType = 'vote';
                    if ((voteType === 'upvote' && isUpvoted) || (voteType === 'downvote' && isDownvoted)) {
                        actionType = 'remove';
                    }
                    
                    // Get current net vote count for optimistic update
                    const netCounters = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-net-count[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    let currentNet = 0;
                    if (netCounters.length > 0) {
                        const currentText = netCounters[0].textContent.trim();
                        // Parse current net count (remove + sign if present)
                        currentNet = parseInt(currentText.replace(/[+,\s]/g, '')) || 0;
                    }
                    
                    // Optimistic UI update
                    if (actionType === 'remove') {
                        // Remove vote
                        if (voteType === 'upvote') {
                            allUpvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.remove('upvoted', 'voted');
                                btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                            });
                            // Update net count optimistically
                            const newNet = currentNet - 1;
                            netCounters.forEach(counter => {
                                const formatted = Math.abs(newNet) >= 1000 ? new Intl.NumberFormat().format(newNet) : newNet.toString();
                                counter.textContent = (newNet > 0 ? '+' : '') + formatted;
                            });
                        } else {
                            allDownvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.remove('downvoted', 'voted');
                                btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                            });
                            // Update net count optimistically
                            const newNet = currentNet + 1;
                            netCounters.forEach(counter => {
                                const formatted = Math.abs(newNet) >= 1000 ? new Intl.NumberFormat().format(newNet) : newNet.toString();
                                counter.textContent = (newNet > 0 ? '+' : '') + formatted;
                            });
                        }
                    } else {
                        // Add vote (remove opposite first)
                        if (voteType === 'upvote') {
                            allUpvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.add('upvoted', 'voted');
                                btn.classList.remove('downvoted');
                                btn.dataset.voted = '1';
                                btn.classList.add('animating');
                                // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                btn.classList.remove('text-gray-600', 'text-red-600');
                                btn.classList.add('text-blue-600');
                                setTimeout(() => btn.classList.remove('animating'), 400);
                            });
                            allDownvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.remove('downvoted', 'voted');
                                btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                            });
                            // Update net count optimistically
                            // If currently downvoted, remove downvote (+1) and add upvote (+1) = +2
                            // If not voted, just add upvote (+1)
                            const wasDownvoted = isDownvoted;
                            const newNet = wasDownvoted ? currentNet + 2 : currentNet + 1;
                            netCounters.forEach(counter => {
                                const formatted = Math.abs(newNet) >= 1000 ? new Intl.NumberFormat().format(newNet) : newNet.toString();
                                counter.textContent = (newNet > 0 ? '+' : '') + formatted;
                            });
                        } else {
                            allDownvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.add('downvoted', 'voted');
                                btn.classList.remove('upvoted');
                                btn.dataset.voted = '1';
                                btn.classList.add('animating');
                                // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                btn.classList.remove('text-gray-600', 'text-blue-600');
                                btn.classList.add('text-red-600');
                                setTimeout(() => btn.classList.remove('animating'), 400);
                            });
                            allUpvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                btn.classList.remove('upvoted', 'voted');
                                btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                            });
                            // Update net count optimistically
                            // If currently upvoted, remove upvote (-1) and add downvote (-1) = -2
                            // If not voted, just add downvote (-1)
                            const wasUpvoted = isUpvoted;
                            const newNet = wasUpvoted ? currentNet - 2 : currentNet - 1;
                            netCounters.forEach(counter => {
                                const formatted = Math.abs(newNet) >= 1000 ? new Intl.NumberFormat().format(newNet) : newNet.toString();
                                counter.textContent = (newNet > 0 ? '+' : '') + formatted;
                            });
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // AJAX call
                    fetch(this.ajaxUrl, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                        },
                        body: new URLSearchParams({
                            action: 'niriv_toggle_vote',
                            nonce: this.nonce,
                            object_id: objectId,
                            object_type: objectType,
                            vote_type: voteType,
                            action_type: actionType
                        })
                    })
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        // Re-enable buttons
                        allVoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                            btn.disabled = false;
                            btn.classList.remove('processing');
                            btn.style.pointerEvents = '';
                        });
                        
                        if (data.success) {
                            // Update counts
                            this.updateVoteCounts(objectId, objectType, data.data);
                            
                            // Update button states based on response
                            if (data.data.vote_type === 'upvote') {
                                allUpvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                    btn.classList.add('upvoted', 'voted');
                                    btn.classList.remove('downvoted');
                                    btn.dataset.voted = '1';
                                    // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                    btn.classList.remove('text-gray-600', 'text-red-600');
                                    btn.classList.add('text-blue-600');
                                });
                                allDownvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                    btn.classList.remove('downvoted', 'voted');
                                    btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                    // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                    btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                    btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                                });
                            } else if (data.data.vote_type === 'downvote') {
                                allDownvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                    btn.classList.add('downvoted', 'voted');
                                    btn.classList.remove('upvoted');
                                    btn.dataset.voted = '1';
                                    // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                    btn.classList.remove('text-gray-600', 'text-blue-600');
                                    btn.classList.add('text-red-600');
                                });
                                allUpvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                    btn.classList.remove('upvoted', 'voted');
                                    btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                    // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                    btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                    btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                                });
                            } else {
                                // No vote
                                allUpvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                    btn.classList.remove('upvoted', 'voted');
                                    btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                    // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                    btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                    btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                                });
                                allDownvoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                                    btn.classList.remove('downvoted', 'voted');
                                    btn.dataset.voted = '0';
                                    // Update visual state for custom buttons
                                    btn.classList.remove('text-blue-600', 'text-red-600');
                                    btn.classList.add('text-gray-600');
                                });
                            }
                            
                            // Show toast
                            if (window.nirivToast) {
                                window.nirivToast.show(data.data.message, 'success', 2000);
                            }
                        } else {
                            // Revert on error - reload page or revert UI
                            if (window.nirivToast) {
                                window.nirivToast.show('Error: ' + data.data.message, 'error', 3000);
                            }
                            // Optionally reload the vote counts
                            this.updateVoteCountsFromServer(objectId, objectType);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        // Re-enable buttons on error
                        allVoteBtns.forEach(btn => {
                            btn.disabled = false;
                            btn.classList.remove('processing');
                            btn.style.pointerEvents = '';
                        });
                        
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log('Vote error: ' + (error?.message || error), 'error');
                        }
                        if (window.nirivToast) {
                            window.nirivToast.show('Network error', 'error', 3000);
                        }
                        // Optionally reload the vote counts
                        this.updateVoteCountsFromServer(objectId, objectType);
                    });
                },
                
                updateVoteCounts: function(objectId, objectType, data) {
                    const upvoteCounters = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-upvote-count[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    const downvoteCounters = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-downvote-count[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    const netCounters = document.querySelectorAll(`.niriv-vote-net-count[data-object-id="${objectId}"][data-object-type="${objectType}"]`);
                    
                    upvoteCounters.forEach(counter => {
                        counter.textContent = new Intl.NumberFormat().format(data.upvotes);
                        
                        // Toggle clickable class based on count
                        if (data.upvotes > 0 && !counter.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                            counter.classList.add('clickable');
                        } else if (data.upvotes === 0 && counter.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                            counter.classList.remove('clickable');
                        }
                    });
                    
                    downvoteCounters.forEach(counter => {
                        counter.textContent = new Intl.NumberFormat().format(data.downvotes);
                        
                        // Toggle clickable class based on count
                        if (data.downvotes > 0 && !counter.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                            counter.classList.add('clickable');
                        } else if (data.downvotes === 0 && counter.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                            counter.classList.remove('clickable');
                        }
                    });
                    
                    netCounters.forEach(counter => {
                        const net = data.net_votes;
                        // Format the number (no commas for small numbers, but keep formatting for large ones)
                        const formatted = Math.abs(net) >= 1000 ? new Intl.NumberFormat().format(net) : net.toString();
                        counter.textContent = (net > 0 ? '+' : '') + formatted;
                        counter.title = 'Net votes: ' + net;
                    });
                },
                
                updateVoteCountsFromServer: function(objectId, objectType) {
                    fetch(this.ajaxUrl, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                        },
                        body: new URLSearchParams({
                            action: 'niriv_get_vote_count',
                            nonce: this.nonce,
                            object_id: objectId,
                            object_type: objectType
                        })
                    })
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        if (data.success) {
                            this.updateVoteCounts(objectId, objectType, data.data);
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log('Error fetching vote counts: ' + (error?.message || error), 'error');
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                showVotedUsers: function(objectId, objectType, voteType) {
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-modal');
                    const body = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-body');
                    
                    if (!modal || !body) return;
                    
                    // Show modal with loading state
                    modal.classList.add('active');
                    body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-voted-users-loading"><div class="niriv-vote-spinner"></div></div>';
                    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                    
                    // Fetch voted users
                    fetch(this.ajaxUrl, {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                        },
                        body: new URLSearchParams({
                            action: 'niriv_get_voted_users',
                            nonce: this.nonce,
                            object_id: objectId,
                            object_type: objectType,
                            vote_type: voteType
                        })
                    })
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        if (data.success) {
                            this.updateModalHeader(data.data, voteType);
                            this.renderVotedUsers(data.data.users);
                        } else {
                            body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-voted-users-empty">Error loading users</div>';
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log('Error fetching voted users: ' + (error?.message || error), 'error');
                        }
                        body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-voted-users-empty">Error loading users</div>';
                    });
                },
                
                updateModalHeader: function(data, voteType) {
                    const titleElement = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-modal-title');
                    const subtitleElement = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-modal-subtitle');
                    
                    if (!titleElement || !subtitleElement) return;
                    
                    const totalCount = data.total_count || 0;
                    const voteTypeLabel = voteType === 'upvote' ? 'Upvoted' : 'Downvoted';
                    
                    // Update title with total count
                    if (totalCount > 0) {
                        titleElement.textContent = `${voteTypeLabel} by ${totalCount.toLocaleString()}`;
                    } else {
                        titleElement.textContent = `${voteTypeLabel} by`;
                    }
                    
                    // Update subtitle
                    if (data.count > 0) {
                        subtitleElement.textContent = `${data.count.toLocaleString()} logged-in user${data.count !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
                    } else {
                        subtitleElement.textContent = `Not ${voteType}d by users yet`;
                    }
                },
                
                renderVotedUsers: function(users) {
                    const body = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-body');
                    if (!body) return;
                    
                    if (!users || users.length === 0) {
                        body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-voted-users-empty">Not voted by users yet</div>';
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    const html = `
                        <div class="niriv-voted-users-list">
                            ${users.map(user => `
                                <div class="niriv-voted-user-item">
                                    <img src="${user.avatar}" alt="${user.name}" class="niriv-voted-user-avatar">
                                    <div class="niriv-voted-user-info">
                                        <a href="${user.profile_url}" class="niriv-voted-user-name">${user.name}</a>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            `).join('')}
                        </div>
                    `;
                    
                    body.innerHTML = html;
                },
                
                closeVotedUsersModal: function() {
                    const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-voted-users-modal');
                    if (modal) {
                        modal.classList.remove('active');
                        document.body.style.overflow = '';
                    }
                }
            };
            
            // Initialize on DOM ready
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => NirivVotingSystem.init());
            } else {
                NirivVotingSystem.init();
            }
            
            // Make it globally accessible
            window.NirivVotingSystem = NirivVotingSystem;
        })();
        </script>

<script>
(function() {
    'use strict';
    
    const UniversalLightbox = {
        lightbox: null,
        imageContainer: null,
        image: null,
        currentIndex: 0,
        images: [],
        zoomLevel: 1,
        isDragging: false,
        dragStart: { x: 0, y: 0 },
        imagePosition: { x: 0, y: 0 },
        touchStart: { x: 0, y: 0 },
        touchStartTime: 0,
        
        init: function() {
            this.lightbox = document.getElementById('niriv-universal-lightbox');
            if (!this.lightbox) return;
            
            this.imageContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-image-container');
            this.image = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-image');
            
            this.bindEvents();
            this.setupSyncListeners();
            this.initLightboxLikersModal();
        },
        
        initLightboxLikersModal: function() {
            const self = this;
            
            // Close button
            const closeBtn = document.querySelector('.niriv-lightbox-likers-modal-close');
            if (closeBtn) {
                closeBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    self.closeLightboxLikersModal();
                });
            }
            
            // Click outside to close
            const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-likers-modal');
            if (modal) {
                modal.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    if (e.target === modal) {
                        self.closeLightboxLikersModal();
                    }
                });
            }
            
            // Escape key to close
            document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Escape' && modal && modal.classList.contains('active')) {
                    self.closeLightboxLikersModal();
                }
            });
        },
        
        setupSyncListeners: function() {
            const self = this;
            
            // Listen to like updates from global like system
            document.addEventListener('niriv_like_updated', function(event) {
                const { postId, likes, user_liked } = event.detail;
                // Only update if this is the post we're showing
                if (self.postId && self.postId == postId && self.lightbox.classList.contains('active')) {
                    const likeContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-like-container');
                    if (likeContainer) {
                        // Button is inside .niriv-like-container div
                        const likeContainerDiv = likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-container');
                        const likeBtn = likeContainerDiv ? likeContainerDiv.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn') : likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn');
                        
                        if (likeBtn) {
                            // Update button state
                            if (user_liked) {
                                likeBtn.classList.add('liked');
                                likeBtn.dataset.liked = '1';
                                likeBtn.style.color = '#ef4444';
                            } else {
                                likeBtn.classList.remove('liked');
                                likeBtn.dataset.liked = '0';
                                likeBtn.style.color = '#6b7280';
                            }
                            
                            const icon = likeBtn.querySelector('.niriv-like-icon');
                            if (icon) {
                                if (user_liked) {
                                    icon.style.fill = '#ef4444';
                                    icon.style.stroke = '#ef4444';
                                    icon.style.color = '#ef4444';
                                } else {
                                    icon.style.fill = 'none';
                                    icon.style.stroke = '#6b7280';
                                    icon.style.color = '#6b7280';
                                }
                            }
                            
                            // Update count - count is sibling of button in .niriv-like-container
                            const containerForCount = likeContainerDiv || likeContainer;
                            let countSpan = containerForCount.querySelector('.niriv-like-count');
                            
                            if (likes > 0) {
                                if (!countSpan) {
                                    countSpan = document.createElement('span');
                                    countSpan.className = 'niriv-like-count clickable';
                                    countSpan.setAttribute('data-post-id', postId);
                                    containerForCount.appendChild(countSpan);
                                }
                                countSpan.textContent = new Intl.NumberFormat().format(likes);
                                countSpan.style.display = 'inline';
                                countSpan.style.visibility = 'visible';
                                countSpan.style.opacity = '1';
                                countSpan.style.marginLeft = '4px';
                            } else if (countSpan) {
                                countSpan.style.display = 'none';
                                countSpan.textContent = '';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            
            // Also listen to updateLikeCounts calls from the global like system
            if (typeof nirivLikeSystem !== 'undefined' && nirivLikeSystem.updateLikeCounts) {
                const originalUpdateLikeCounts = nirivLikeSystem.updateLikeCounts;
                nirivLikeSystem.updateLikeCounts = function(postId, count) {
                    // Call original function
                    originalUpdateLikeCounts.call(this, postId, count);
                    
                    // Also update lightbox if it's open and showing this post
                    if (self.postId && self.postId == postId && self.lightbox.classList.contains('active')) {
                        const likeContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-like-container');
                        if (likeContainer) {
                            // Button is inside .niriv-like-container div
                            const likeContainerDiv = likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-container');
                            const containerForCount = likeContainerDiv || likeContainer;
                            
                            // Count is sibling of button in .niriv-like-container
                            let countSpan = containerForCount.querySelector('.niriv-like-count');
                            
                            if (count > 0) {
                                if (!countSpan) {
                                    countSpan = document.createElement('span');
                                    countSpan.className = 'niriv-like-count clickable';
                                    countSpan.setAttribute('data-post-id', postId);
                                    containerForCount.appendChild(countSpan);
                                }
                                countSpan.textContent = new Intl.NumberFormat().format(count);
                                countSpan.style.display = 'inline';
                                countSpan.style.visibility = 'visible';
                                countSpan.style.opacity = '1';
                                countSpan.style.marginLeft = '4px';
                                if (!countSpan.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                                    countSpan.classList.add('clickable');
                                }
                            } else if (countSpan) {
                                countSpan.style.display = 'none';
                                countSpan.textContent = '';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };
            }
        },
        
        bindEvents: function() {
            const self = this;
            
            // Close button
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-close').addEventListener('click', () => this.close());
            
            // Navigation buttons
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-prev').addEventListener('click', () => this.prev());
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-next').addEventListener('click', () => this.next());
            
            // Zoom buttons
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-zoom-in').addEventListener('click', () => this.zoomIn());
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-zoom-out').addEventListener('click', () => this.zoomOut());
            
            // Download button
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-download').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                e.preventDefault();
                this.download();
            });
            
            // Click outside to close
            this.lightbox.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                if (e.target === this.lightbox || e.target === this.lightbox.querySelector('.niriv-lightbox-wrapper')) {
                    this.close();
                }
            });
            
            // Handle cafe-lightbox-trigger clicks (global event delegation)
            document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const trigger = e.target.closest('.cafe-lightbox-trigger');
                if (trigger) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    try {
                        const galleryData = trigger.dataset.gallery;
                        const parsedData = galleryData ? JSON.parse(galleryData) : [];
                        const startIndex = parseInt(trigger.dataset.index) || 0;
                        
                        // Convert to universal lightbox format
                        const images = parsedData.map(img => ({
                            url: img.url || img.src,
                            src: img.url || img.src,
                            thumbnail: img.thumbnail || img.url || img.src,
                            caption: img.caption || img.title || ''
                        }));
                        
                        // Get post ID from trigger element or closest parent
                        let postId = null;
                        const triggerPostId = trigger.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                        if (triggerPostId) {
                            const numId = parseInt(triggerPostId, 10);
                            if (!isNaN(numId) && numId > 0) {
                                postId = numId;
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // If not on trigger, check closest parent
                        if (!postId) {
                            const parentWithPostId = trigger.closest('[data-post-id]');
                            if (parentWithPostId) {
                                const parentPostId = parentWithPostId.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                                if (parentPostId) {
                                    const numId = parseInt(parentPostId, 10);
                                    if (!isNaN(numId) && numId > 0) {
                                        postId = numId;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // Open universal lightbox using self reference
                        self.open(images, startIndex, {
                            caption: images[startIndex]?.caption || '',
                            postId: postId,
                            triggerElement: trigger
                        });
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Lightbox: Failed to parse gallery data:', error);
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log('Failed to open lightbox: ' + (error?.message || error), 'error');
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            
            // Keyboard navigation
            document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
                if (!this.lightbox.classList.contains('active')) return;
                
                switch(e.key) {
                    case 'Escape':
                        this.close();
                        break;
                    case 'ArrowLeft':
                        this.prev();
                        break;
                    case 'ArrowRight':
                        this.next();
                        break;
                    case '+':
                    case '=':
                        e.preventDefault();
                        this.zoomIn();
                        break;
                    case '-':
                        e.preventDefault();
                        this.zoomOut();
                        break;
                }
            });
            
            // Mouse wheel zoom
            this.imageContainer.addEventListener('wheel', (e) => {
                if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    if (e.deltaY < 0) {
                        this.zoomIn();
                    } else {
                        this.zoomOut();
                    }
                }
            }, { passive: false });
            
            // Touch events for mobile swipe - improved detection
            let touchStartX = 0;
            let touchStartY = 0;
            let touchStartTime = 0;
            let isSwiping = false;
            let hasMoved = false;
            
            // Prevent swipe when zoomed
            this.imageContainer.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
                if (self.zoomLevel > 1) {
                    return; // Don't handle swipe when zoomed
                }
                touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                touchStartTime = Date.now();
                isSwiping = false;
                hasMoved = false;
            }, { passive: true });
            
            this.imageContainer.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
                if (self.zoomLevel > 1) {
                    return; // Don't handle swipe when zoomed
                }
                if (!touchStartX) return;
                
                const touchCurrentX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                const touchCurrentY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                const deltaX = touchCurrentX - touchStartX;
                const deltaY = touchCurrentY - touchStartY;
                
                // Check if horizontal movement is greater than vertical (swipe, not scroll)
                if (Math.abs(deltaX) > 10 && Math.abs(deltaX) > Math.abs(deltaY)) {
                    hasMoved = true;
                    isSwiping = true;
                    // Prevent default scrolling while swiping
                    e.preventDefault();
                }
            }, { passive: false });
            
            this.imageContainer.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
                if (self.zoomLevel > 1) {
                    return; // Don't handle swipe when zoomed
                }
                if (!touchStartX || !hasMoved) {
                    touchStartX = 0;
                    return;
                }
                
                const touchEndX = e.changedTouches[0].clientX;
                const touchEndY = e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
                const deltaX = touchEndX - touchStartX;
                const deltaY = touchEndY - touchStartY;
                const deltaTime = Date.now() - touchStartTime;
                const distance = Math.abs(deltaX);
                
                // Improved swipe detection: faster, more distance, clearly horizontal
                if (isSwiping && deltaTime < 400 && distance > 80 && Math.abs(deltaX) > Math.abs(deltaY) * 2) {
                    if (deltaX > 0) {
                        // Swipe right - previous
                        self.prev();
                    } else {
                        // Swipe left - next
                        self.next();
                    }
                }
                
                // Reset
                touchStartX = 0;
                touchStartY = 0;
                isSwiping = false;
                hasMoved = false;
            }, { passive: true });
            
            // Image drag for zoomed images
            this.imageContainer.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
                if (this.zoomLevel > 1) {
                    this.isDragging = true;
                    this.dragStart.x = e.clientX - this.imagePosition.x;
                    this.dragStart.y = e.clientY - this.imagePosition.y;
                    this.imageContainer.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
                }
            });
            
            document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
                if (this.isDragging && this.zoomLevel > 1) {
                    this.imagePosition.x = e.clientX - this.dragStart.x;
                    this.imagePosition.y = e.clientY - this.dragStart.y;
                    this.updateImageTransform();
                }
            });
            
            document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
                if (this.isDragging) {
                    this.isDragging = false;
                    this.imageContainer.style.cursor = 'move';
                }
            });
        },
        
        open: function(images, startIndex = 0, options = {}) {
            this.images = images;
            this.currentIndex = startIndex;
            this.zoomLevel = 1;
            this.imagePosition = { x: 0, y: 0 };
            
            // Get post ID - improved detection
            // Priority: 1) options.postId, 2) trigger's data-post-id, 3) closest parent with data-post-id
            let postId = options.postId || null;
            
            // If postId is provided, ensure it's numeric
            if (postId) {
                if (typeof postId === 'string') {
                    // Try to parse as number first
                    const numId = parseInt(postId, 10);
                    if (!isNaN(numId) && numId > 0) {
                        postId = numId;
                    } else {
                        // If it's a URL, try to extract ID
                        const urlMatch = postId.match(/[?&]p=(\d+)/);
                        if (urlMatch) {
                            postId = parseInt(urlMatch[1], 10);
                        } else {
                            postId = null;
                        }
                    }
                } else if (typeof postId === 'number' && postId > 0) {
                    postId = postId;
                } else {
                    postId = null;
                }
            }
            
            // If still no postId, get from trigger element
            // Priority: 1) .cafe-photo-post container (most reliable), 2) trigger's data-post-id, 3) any parent with data-post-id
            if (!postId || postId === 0) {
                if (options.triggerElement) {
                    const trigger = options.triggerElement;
                    
                    // Strategy 1: Check closest .cafe-photo-post container FIRST (most reliable source)
                    let foundPostId = null;
                    const cafePostContainer = trigger.closest('.cafe-photo-post');
                    if (cafePostContainer) {
                        foundPostId = cafePostContainer.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                        if (foundPostId) {
                            const numId = parseInt(foundPostId, 10);
                            if (!isNaN(numId) && numId > 0) {
                                postId = numId;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Strategy 2: Check trigger element itself (fallback)
                    if (!postId || postId === 0) {
                        foundPostId = trigger.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                        if (foundPostId) {
                            const numId = parseInt(foundPostId, 10);
                            if (!isNaN(numId) && numId > 0) {
                                postId = numId;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Strategy 3: Check any parent with data-post-id (final fallback)
                    if (!postId || postId === 0) {
                        const parentWithPostId = trigger.closest('[data-post-id]');
                        if (parentWithPostId && parentWithPostId !== trigger) {
                            foundPostId = parentWithPostId.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                            if (foundPostId) {
                                const numId = parseInt(foundPostId, 10);
                                if (!isNaN(numId) && numId > 0) {
