                                    postId = numId;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            this.postId = postId && !isNaN(postId) && postId > 0 ? postId : null;
            
            // Store original post ID - this should NOT change when switching images
            // All images in the gallery belong to the same post
            // Sidebar data (likes, comments, share) should remain the same for all images
            this.originalPostId = this.postId;
            
            // Show lightbox
            this.lightbox.classList.add('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            
            // Show image
            this.showImage(this.currentIndex);
            
            // Build thumbnails
            this.buildThumbnails();
            
            // Load like button, comments, share, author, and caption if post ID is available
            if (this.postId) {
                this.loadPostData(this.postId);
            } else {
                // Fallback to provided data - try to get post title from page
                const captionEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-caption');
                if (captionEl) {
                    // Try to get post title from the page
                    let titleText = '';
                    const postTitleEl = document.querySelector('h1, .entry-title, .post-title, article h1');
                    if (postTitleEl) {
                        titleText = postTitleEl.textContent || postTitleEl.innerText || '';
                    }
                    
                    // Fall back to provided caption if no title found
                    if (!titleText && options.caption !== undefined) {
                        titleText = options.caption || '';
                    }
                    
                    if (titleText) {
                        // Decode HTML entities
                        const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
                        textarea.innerHTML = titleText;
                        titleText = textarea.value;
                        
                        // Process hashtags in title
                        let titleHtml = titleText;
                        // Replace hashtags with clickable links
                        titleHtml = titleHtml.replace(/#(\w+)/g, function(match, tag) {
                            const hashtagUrl = 'https://www.niriv.com/hashtag/' + encodeURIComponent(tag.toLowerCase());
                            return '<a href="' + hashtagUrl + '" class="niriv-hashtag" data-tag="' + tag + '" style="color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 500; text-decoration: none;">#' + tag + '</a>';
                        });
                        captionEl.innerHTML = titleHtml;
                    } else {
                        captionEl.textContent = '';
                    }
                }
                
                const commentCountEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-count');
                if (commentCountEl && options.commentCount !== undefined) {
                    commentCountEl.textContent = options.commentCount || 0;
                }
                
                if (options.comments && Array.isArray(options.comments)) {
                    this.renderComments(options.comments.slice(0, 4));
                    const loadMoreEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-load-more');
                    if (loadMoreEl) {
                        loadMoreEl.style.display = options.comments.length > 4 ? 'block' : 'none';
                    }
                }
            }
        },
        
        loadPostData: function(postId) {
            const self = this;
            
            // Use original post ID if available (preserved from when lightbox opened)
            // This ensures sidebar data stays the same when switching images
            if (!postId && this.originalPostId) {
                postId = this.originalPostId;
            }
            
            // Store post ID for use throughout lightbox session
            this.postId = postId;
            
            if (!postId) {
                console.warn('Lightbox: No post ID available for loading post data');
                return;
            }
            
            // Update like button post ID (button already rendered by PHP)
            const likeContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-like-container');
            if (likeContainer && postId) {
                // Button is inside .niriv-like-container div (from PHP render function)
                const likeContainerDiv = likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-container');
                const likeBtn = likeContainerDiv ? likeContainerDiv.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn') : likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn');
                
                if (likeBtn) {
                    // Update post ID
                    likeBtn.setAttribute('data-post-id', String(postId));
                    
                    // Attach click handler (only if not already attached)
                    if (!likeBtn.hasAttribute('data-handler-attached')) {
                        likeBtn.setAttribute('data-handler-attached', 'true');
                        
                        // Attach click listener
                        if (typeof nirivLikeSystem !== 'undefined' && nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike) {
                            likeBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                e.stopPropagation();
                                nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike(likeBtn);
                            });
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            // Load like data via AJAX and update button
            // Use URLSearchParams like feed-data-fetcher.js does for consistency
            const params = new URLSearchParams();
            params.append('action', 'niriv_get_like_counts');
            params.append('post_ids[]', String(postId)); // Send as array element
            params.append('nonce', 'a27bec8f1e');
            
            fetch('https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                },
                body: params
            })
            .then(response => {
                // Check if response is OK
                if (!response.ok) {
                    return response.text().then(text => {
                        console.error('Lightbox: HTTP error', response.status, text.substring(0, 200));
                        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
                    });
                }
                // Check content type
                const contentType = response.headers.get('content-type');
                if (!contentType || !contentType.includes('application/json')) {
                    return response.text().then(text => {
                        console.error('Lightbox: Expected JSON but got:', text.substring(0, 200));
                        throw new Error('Response is not JSON');
                    });
                }
                return response.json();
            })
            .then(data => {
                console.log('Lightbox: Like data response', { postId, data });
                
                const likeContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-like-container');
                if (!likeContainer) {
                    console.warn('Lightbox: Like container not found');
                    return;
                }
                
                let isLiked = false;
                let likeCount = 0;
                
                if (data.success && data.data) {
                    // Check if data is an object with post IDs as keys
                    if (data.data[postId]) {
                        const likeData = data.data[postId];
                        isLiked = likeData.user_liked || false;
                        likeCount = likeData.count || 0;
                        console.log('Lightbox: Like data loaded', { postId, isLiked, likeCount, likeData });
                    } else if (data.data.count !== undefined) {
                        // Fallback: direct count property
                        likeCount = data.data.count || 0;
                        isLiked = data.data.user_liked || false;
                        console.log('Lightbox: Like data (fallback)', { postId, isLiked, likeCount });
                    } else {
                        console.warn('Lightbox: Unexpected like data format', data);
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn('Lightbox: Failed to load like data', data);
                }
                
                // Update like button with data
                // The button is inside a .niriv-like-container div (from PHP render)
                const likeContainerDiv = likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-container');
                const likeBtn = likeContainerDiv ? likeContainerDiv.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn') : likeContainer.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn');
                
                console.log('Lightbox: Finding like button', { 
                    hasContainer: !!likeContainer, 
                    hasContainerDiv: !!likeContainerDiv,
                    hasButton: !!likeBtn,
                    containerHTML: likeContainer ? likeContainer.innerHTML.substring(0, 200) : 'none'
                });
                
                if (likeBtn) {
                    // Update post ID
                    likeBtn.setAttribute('data-post-id', String(postId));
                    
                    // Update liked state - apply both class and inline styles for reliability
                    if (isLiked) {
                        likeBtn.classList.add('liked');
                        likeBtn.dataset.liked = '1';
                        likeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Unlike');
                        // Apply inline styles as fallback
                        likeBtn.style.color = '#ef4444';
                    } else {
                        likeBtn.classList.remove('liked');
                        likeBtn.dataset.liked = '0';
                        likeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Like');
                        // Apply inline styles as fallback
                        likeBtn.style.color = '#6b7280';
                    }
                    
                    // Update icon styles
                    const icon = likeBtn.querySelector('.niriv-like-icon');
                    if (icon) {
                        if (isLiked) {
                            icon.style.fill = '#ef4444';
                            icon.style.stroke = '#ef4444';
                            icon.style.color = '#ef4444';
                        } else {
                            icon.style.fill = 'none';
                            icon.style.stroke = '#6b7280';
                            icon.style.color = '#6b7280';
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Update or add like count - count is sibling of button in .niriv-like-container
                    const containerForCount = likeContainerDiv || likeContainer;
                    let countSpan = containerForCount.querySelector('.niriv-like-count');
                    
                    // Always create count span if it doesn't exist (even if count is 0)
                    if (!countSpan) {
                        countSpan = document.createElement('span');
                        countSpan.className = 'niriv-like-count';
                        countSpan.setAttribute('data-post-id', postId);
                        // Insert after the button
                        if (likeBtn.nextSibling) {
                            containerForCount.insertBefore(countSpan, likeBtn.nextSibling);
                        } else {
                            containerForCount.appendChild(countSpan);
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Update count span attributes
                    countSpan.setAttribute('data-post-id', postId);
                    
                    if (likeCount > 0) {
                        countSpan.textContent = new Intl.NumberFormat().format(likeCount);
                        // Explicitly set display to inline with !important (override any previous none)
                        countSpan.style.setProperty('display', 'inline', 'important');
                        countSpan.style.setProperty('visibility', 'visible', 'important');
                        countSpan.style.setProperty('opacity', '1', 'important');
                        countSpan.style.marginLeft = '4px';
                        if (!countSpan.classList.contains('clickable')) {
                            countSpan.classList.add('clickable');
                        }
                        // Add click handler to show custom lightbox modal above the counter
                        if (!countSpan.hasAttribute('data-lightbox-handler')) {
                            countSpan.setAttribute('data-lightbox-handler', 'true');
                            countSpan.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                e.preventDefault();
                                e.stopPropagation();
                                const postId = this.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                                if (postId) {
                                    self.showLightboxLikersModal(postId, this);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                        // Force show with attribute
                        countSpan.setAttribute('data-count', likeCount);
                        countSpan.removeAttribute('data-hidden');
                    } else {
                        // Hide count span but keep it for future updates
                        countSpan.style.setProperty('display', 'none', 'important');
                        countSpan.style.setProperty('visibility', 'hidden', 'important');
                        countSpan.style.setProperty('opacity', '0', 'important');
                        countSpan.textContent = '';
                        countSpan.removeAttribute('data-count');
                        countSpan.setAttribute('data-hidden', 'true');
                    }
                    
                    // Force a reflow to ensure styles are applied
                    void likeBtn.offsetHeight;
                    if (countSpan) void countSpan.offsetHeight;
                    
                    console.log('Lightbox: Updated like button', { 
                        postId, 
                        isLiked, 
                        likeCount, 
                        hasCountSpan: !!countSpan,
                        countDisplay: countSpan ? countSpan.style.display : 'none',
                        countText: countSpan ? countSpan.textContent : '',
                        countVisible: countSpan ? window.getComputedStyle(countSpan).display !== 'none' : false,
                        buttonClasses: likeBtn.className,
                        buttonLiked: likeBtn.dataset.liked,
                        buttonHasLikedClass: likeBtn.classList.contains('liked'),
                        buttonColor: window.getComputedStyle(likeBtn).color,
                        buttonInlineColor: likeBtn.style.color,
                        iconFill: icon ? window.getComputedStyle(icon).fill : 'none',
                        iconStroke: icon ? window.getComputedStyle(icon).stroke : 'none',
                        iconInlineFill: icon ? icon.style.fill : 'none',
                        iconInlineStroke: icon ? icon.style.stroke : 'none'
                    });
                } else {
                    console.warn('Lightbox: Like button not found', { 
                        likeContainer, 
                        likeContainerDiv,
                        hasContainer: !!likeContainer,
                        containerHTML: likeContainer ? likeContainer.innerHTML.substring(0, 300) : 'none'
                    });
                }
            })
            .catch(error => {
                console.error('Error loading like data:', error);
                // Button already shown, just leave it as is
            });
            
            // Comment count will be loaded with comments (no separate call needed)
            
            // Load post metadata (author, caption, date) via AJAX
            fetch('https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
                },
                body: 'action=niriv_get_post_meta&post_id=' + postId + '&nonce=a27bec8f1e'
            })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success && data.data) {
                    // Load author info
                    const authorMeta = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-author-meta');
                    const authorAvatar = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-author-avatar');
                    const authorName = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-author-name');
                    const postDate = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-post-date');
                    
                    if (data.data.author) {
                        if (authorMeta) authorMeta.style.display = 'flex';
                        if (authorAvatar && data.data.author.avatar) {
                            authorAvatar.src = data.data.author.avatar;
                            authorAvatar.alt = data.data.author.name || '';
                        }
                        if (authorName) {
                            if (data.data.author.url) {
                                authorName.innerHTML = '<a href="' + data.data.author.url + '">' + (data.data.author.name || 'Unknown') + '</a>';
                            } else {
                                authorName.textContent = data.data.author.name || 'Unknown';
                            }
                        }
                        if (postDate && data.data.date) {
                            postDate.textContent = data.data.date;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Load post title (instead of caption) with hashtag linking
                    const captionEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-caption');
                    if (captionEl) {
                        // Use post title if available, otherwise fall back to caption
                        let titleText = data.data.title || data.data.caption || '';
                        if (titleText) {
                            // Decode HTML entities
                            const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
                            textarea.innerHTML = titleText;
                            titleText = textarea.value;
                            
                            // Process hashtags in title
                            let titleHtml = titleText;
                            // Replace hashtags with clickable links
                            titleHtml = titleHtml.replace(/#(\w+)/g, function(match, tag) {
                                const hashtagUrl = 'https://www.niriv.com/hashtag/' + encodeURIComponent(tag.toLowerCase());
                                return '<a href="' + hashtagUrl + '" class="niriv-hashtag" data-tag="' + tag + '" style="color: #3b82f6; font-weight: 500; text-decoration: none;">#' + tag + '</a>';
                            });
                            captionEl.innerHTML = titleHtml;
                        } else {
                            captionEl.textContent = '';
                        }
                    }
                }
            })
            .catch(error => {
                console.error('Error loading post metadata:', error);
            });
            
            // Load comments
            this.loadComments(postId, 1, 4);
            
            // Set share button post ID and attach handler
            const shareBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-share');
            if (shareBtn) {
                shareBtn.setAttribute('data-post-id', postId);
                // Use existing share handler if available
                shareBtn.onclick = function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    if (typeof handleInteraction === 'function') {
                        handleInteraction('share', postId, shareBtn);
                    } else {
                        // Fallback: copy link to clipboard
                        const postUrl = 'https://www.niriv.com/?p=' + postId;
                        navigator.clipboard.writeText(postUrl).then(() => {
                            if (window.nirivToast) {
                                window.nirivToast.show('Link copied to clipboard', 'success', 2000);
                            }
                        }).catch(() => {
                            // Fallback for older browsers
                            const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
                            textarea.value = postUrl;
                            document.body.appendChild(textarea);
                            textarea.select();
                            document.execCommand('copy');
                            document.body.removeChild(textarea);
                            if (window.nirivToast) {
                                window.nirivToast.show('Link copied to clipboard', 'success', 2000);
                            }
                        });
                    }
                };
            }
            
            // Set comment button - don't link, just show count
            const commentBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-btn');
            if (commentBtn) {
                // Remove href to prevent navigation
                commentBtn.removeAttribute('href');
                commentBtn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                
                // Check if mobile (use matchMedia for better detection)
                const checkMobile = () => window.innerWidth <= 768;
                
                commentBtn.onclick = function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    
                    if (checkMobile()) {
                        // On mobile, open comment modal using data attribute
                        const postId = self.postId || self.originalPostId;
                        if (postId) {
                            // Create a temporary trigger element with data-open-comments
                            const trigger = document.createElement('button');
                            trigger.setAttribute('data-open-comments', postId);
                            trigger.style.display = 'none';
                            document.body.appendChild(trigger);
                            // Trigger click which will be caught by comment modal listener
                            trigger.click();
                            setTimeout(() => trigger.remove(), 100);
                        }
                    } else {
                        // On desktop, comments are shown in sidebar (no action needed)
                    }
                };
            }
            
            // Initialize comment form handler
            this.initCommentForm();
        },
        
        initCommentForm: function() {
            const self = this;
            const commentForm = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-form');
            const commentInput = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-input');
            
            if (!commentForm || !commentInput) {
                console.warn('Lightbox: Comment form elements not found');
                return;
            }
            
            // Remove existing event listeners by cloning the form (prevents duplicate handlers)
            const formParent = commentForm.parentNode;
            const newForm = commentForm.cloneNode(true);
            formParent.replaceChild(newForm, commentForm);
            
            // Get the new input element
            const newInput = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-input');
            if (!newInput) {
                console.warn('Lightbox: Comment input not found after cloning');
                return;
            }
            
            // Check if user is logged in
            const isLoggedIn = false;
            if (!isLoggedIn) {
                newInput.placeholder = 'Log in to comment';
                newInput.readOnly = true;
                newForm.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    window.location.href = 'https://www.niriv.com/nid?redirect_to=' + encodeURIComponent(window.location.href);
                });
                return;
            }
            
            // Enable input for logged-in users
            newInput.readOnly = false;
            newInput.placeholder = 'Write your comment';
            
            newForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                
                if (!self.postId) {
                    console.warn('Lightbox: No post ID available for commenting');
                    if (window.nirivNotify) {
                        window.nirivNotify.log('Unable to post comment: No post ID', 'error');
                    }
                    return;
                }
                
                const commentText = newInput.value.trim();
                if (!commentText) return;
                
                // Clear input immediately
                newInput.value = '';
                
                // Disable submit button
                const submitBtn = newForm.querySelector('.niriv-lightbox-composer-send');
                if (submitBtn) {
                    submitBtn.disabled = true;
                }
                
                // Add optimistic comment
                self.addOptimisticComment({
                    author: 'You',
                    text: commentText,
                    timestamp: 'Just now',
                    avatar: ''
                });
                
                // Submit comment (use same format as comment modal)
                const formData = new FormData();
                formData.set('action', 'niriv_submit_comment');
                formData.set('nonce', 'c5e2279643');
                formData.set('comment_post_ID', String(self.postId));
                formData.set('comment_parent', '0');
                formData.set('comment', commentText);
                
                fetch('https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    body: formData
                })
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    // Re-enable submit button
                    if (submitBtn) {
                        submitBtn.disabled = false;
                    }
                    
                    if (data.success) {
                        // Remove optimistic comment
                        self.removeOptimisticComment();
                        
                        // Reload comments to show the real one
                        self.loadComments(self.postId, 1, 4);
                        
                        // Update comment count from response
                        if (data.data && data.data.count !== undefined) {
                            const commentCountEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-count');
                            if (commentCountEl) {
                                const count = data.data.count || 0;
                                if (count > 0) {
                                    commentCountEl.textContent = count;
                                    commentCountEl.style.display = 'inline';
                                } else {
                                    commentCountEl.style.display = 'none';
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // Scroll to top of comments to show new comment
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comments');
                            if (commentsContainer) {
                                commentsContainer.scrollTop = 0;
                            }
                        }, 100);
                    } else {
                        // Remove optimistic comment on error
                        self.removeOptimisticComment();
                        if (window.nirivNotify) {
                            window.nirivNotify.log(data.data?.message || 'Failed to post comment', 'error');
                        } else {
                            alert(data.data?.message || 'Failed to post comment');
                        }
                        // Restore input
                        newInput.value = commentText;
                    }
                })
                .catch(error => {
                    // Re-enable submit button
                    if (submitBtn) {
                        submitBtn.disabled = false;
                    }
                    // Remove optimistic comment on error
                    self.removeOptimisticComment();
                    console.error('Error submitting comment:', error);
                    if (window.nirivNotify) {
                        window.nirivNotify.log('Network error', 'error');
                    } else {
                        alert('Network error');
                    }
                    // Restore input
                    newInput.value = commentText;
                });
            });
        },
        
        addOptimisticComment: function(comment) {
            const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comments');
            if (!commentsContainer) return;
            
            // Remove "No comments yet" message if exists
            const noCommentsMsg = commentsContainer.querySelector('p');
            if (noCommentsMsg && noCommentsMsg.textContent.includes('No comments')) {
                noCommentsMsg.remove();
            }
            
            const tempId = 'temp-comment-' + Date.now();
            const optimisticHtml = `
                <div id="${tempId}" class="niriv-lightbox-comment optimistic-comment" style="opacity: 0.7; padding: 12px 20px; border-bottom: 1px solid #e5e7eb;">
                    <div style="display: flex; gap: 12px;">
                        <div style="flex-shrink: 0;">
                            ${comment.avatar ? `<img src="${comment.avatar}" alt="${comment.author}" style="width: 32px; height: 32px; border-radius: 50%;">` : '<div style="width: 32px; height: 32px; border-radius: 50%; background: #e5e7eb;"></div>'}
                        </div>
                        <div style="flex: 1; min-width: 0;">
                            <div style="display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; margin-bottom: 4px;">
                                <span style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: 700; color: #050505;">${comment.author}</span>
                                <span style="font-size: 12px; color: #65676b;">you</span>
                                <span style="font-size: 12px; color: #65676b; margin-left: auto;">${comment.timestamp}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div style="font-size: 15px; color: #050505; line-height: 1.4; word-wrap: break-word;">
                                ${comment.text}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            
            commentsContainer.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', optimisticHtml);
            
            // Update comment count optimistically
            const commentCountEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-count');
            if (commentCountEl) {
                const currentCount = parseInt(commentCountEl.textContent) || 0;
                commentCountEl.textContent = currentCount + 1;
                commentCountEl.style.display = 'inline';
            }
        },
        
        removeOptimisticComment: function() {
            const optimistic = document.querySelector('.optimistic-comment');
            if (optimistic) {
                optimistic.remove();
            }
        },
        
        updateCommentCount: function() {
            if (!this.postId) return;
            
            const commentCountEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-count');
            if (!commentCountEl) return;
            
            // Use same format as comment modal
            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('action', 'niriv_get_comments');
            formData.append('nonce', 'c5e2279643');
            formData.append('post_id', String(this.postId));
            
            fetch('https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success && data.data) {
                    const count = data.data.count || 0;
                    if (count > 0) {
                        commentCountEl.textContent = count;
                        commentCountEl.style.display = 'inline';
                    } else {
                        commentCountEl.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }
            })
            .catch(error => console.error('Error updating comment count:', error));
        },
        
        showLightboxLikersModal: function(postId, counterElement) {
            const self = this;
            const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-likers-modal');
            const modalContent = modal?.querySelector('.niriv-lightbox-likers-modal-content');
            const body = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-likers-body');
            
            if (!modal || !body) return;
            
            // Lock body scroll
            const scrollY = window.scrollY;
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            document.body.style.position = 'fixed';
            document.body.style.width = '100%';
            document.body.style.top = `-${scrollY}px`;
            
            // Show modal
            modal.classList.add('active');
            body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-lightbox-likers-loading"><div class="niriv-spinner-small"></div></div>';
            
            // Position modal above the counter
            if (modalContent && counterElement) {
                const rect = counterElement.getBoundingClientRect();
                const modalHeight = 400; // Max height
                const topPosition = rect.top - modalHeight - 20; // 20px gap above
                
                // Position modal content
                modalContent.style.position = 'fixed';
                
                if (topPosition < 20) {
                    // Position at top with margin
                    modalContent.style.top = '20px';
                } else {
                    // Position above the counter
                    modalContent.style.top = topPosition + 'px';
                }
                
                // Center horizontally relative to counter
                const modalWidth = 280;
                const leftPosition = rect.left + (rect.width / 2) - (modalWidth / 2);
                
                // Keep within viewport bounds
                const maxLeft = window.innerWidth - modalWidth - 20;
                const finalLeft = Math.max(20, Math.min(leftPosition, maxLeft));
                
                modalContent.style.left = finalLeft + 'px';
            }
            
            // Fetch liked users
            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('action', 'niriv_get_liked_users');
            formData.append('nonce', '0d3d305449');
            formData.append('post_id', String(postId));
            
            fetch('https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success && data.data && data.data.users) {
                    self.renderLightboxLikers(data.data.users);
                } else {
                    body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-lightbox-likers-empty">No likes yet</div>';
                }
            })
            .catch(error => {
                console.error('Error fetching liked users:', error);
                body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-lightbox-likers-empty">Error loading users</div>';
            });
        },
        
        renderLightboxLikers: function(users) {
            const body = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-likers-body');
            if (!body) return;
            
            if (!users || users.length === 0) {
                body.innerHTML = '<div class="niriv-lightbox-likers-empty">No likes yet</div>';
                return;
            }
            
            let html = '';
            users.forEach(user => {
                const avatar = user.avatar || '';
                const name = user.name || 'Unknown';
                const profileUrl = user.profile_url || '#';
                
                html += `
                    <a href="${profileUrl}" class="niriv-lightbox-liker-item">
                        ${avatar ? `<img src="${avatar}" alt="${name}" class="niriv-lightbox-liker-avatar" onerror="this.style.display='none'; this.nextElementSibling.style.display='flex';">` : ''}
                        <div style="display: ${avatar ? 'none' : 'flex'}; width: 32px; height: 32px; border-radius: 50%; background: #e5e7eb; align-items: center; justify-content: center; color: #9ca3af; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 600; flex-shrink: 0;">${name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>
                        <span class="niriv-lightbox-liker-name">${name}</span>
                    </a>
                `;
            });
            
            body.innerHTML = html;
        },
        
        closeLightboxLikersModal: function() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-likers-modal');
            if (modal) {
                modal.classList.remove('active');
                
                // Restore body scroll
                const scrollY = document.body.style.top;
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
                document.body.style.position = '';
                document.body.style.width = '';
                document.body.style.top = '';
                
                if (scrollY) {
                    window.scrollTo(0, parseInt(scrollY || '0') * -1);
                }
            }
        },
        
        loadComments: function(postId, page = 1, perPage = 4) {
            const self = this;
            const commentsContainer = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comments');
            if (!commentsContainer) return;
            
            // Use same format as comment modal - get HTML directly
            const formData = new FormData();
            formData.append('action', 'niriv_get_comments');
            formData.append('nonce', 'c5e2279643');
            formData.append('post_id', String(postId));
            
            fetch('https://www.niriv.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
                method: 'POST',
                body: formData
            })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success && data.data) {
                    // Use HTML directly like comment modal does
                    const html = data.data.html || '';
                    if (html) {
                        // Extract just the list items from the HTML (remove outer ol tags)
                        const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
                        tempDiv.innerHTML = html;
                        const commentList = tempDiv.querySelector('ol.niriv-comment-list, ol');
                        if (commentList) {
                            // Get only the first 4 comments for lightbox
                            const allComments = commentList.querySelectorAll('li');
                            const limitedComments = Array.from(allComments).slice(0, perPage);
                            
                            if (limitedComments.length > 0) {
                                const limitedHtml = '<ol class="niriv-lightbox-comment-list" style="list-style: none; padding: 0; margin: 0;">' + 
                                    limitedComments.map(li => li.outerHTML).join('') + 
                                    '</ol>';
                                commentsContainer.innerHTML = limitedHtml;
                                
                                // Reinitialize like buttons in comments (they're already rendered by PHP)
                                setTimeout(() => {
                                    const commentLikeButtons = commentsContainer.querySelectorAll('.niriv-like-btn');
                                    commentLikeButtons.forEach(btn => {
                                        if (!btn.hasAttribute('data-handler-attached')) {
                                            btn.setAttribute('data-handler-attached', 'true');
                                            if (typeof nirivLikeSystem !== 'undefined' && nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike) {
                                                btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                                    e.preventDefault();
                                                    e.stopPropagation();
                                                    nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike(btn);
                                                });
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                    
                                    // Add click handlers for comment like counters to show lightbox likers modal
                                    const commentLikeCounts = commentsContainer.querySelectorAll('.comment-like-wrapper .niriv-like-count');
                                    commentLikeCounts.forEach(countSpan => {
                                        if (!countSpan.hasAttribute('data-lightbox-handler')) {
                                            countSpan.setAttribute('data-lightbox-handler', 'true');
                                            countSpan.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                                            countSpan.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                                e.preventDefault();
                                                e.stopPropagation();
                                                // Get comment like ID from the like button
                                                const likeBtn = this.closest('.comment-like-wrapper')?.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn');
                                                if (likeBtn) {
                                                    const commentLikeId = likeBtn.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                                                    if (commentLikeId) {
                                                        self.showLightboxLikersModal(commentLikeId, this);
                                                    }
                                                }
                                            });
                                        }
                                    });
                                }, 100);
                                
                                // Show load more if there are more comments
                                const loadMoreEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-load-more');
                                if (loadMoreEl) {
                                    loadMoreEl.style.display = allComments.length > perPage ? 'block' : 'none';
                                    if (allComments.length > perPage) {
                                        loadMoreEl.onclick = () => {
                                            // Load all comments
                                            commentsContainer.innerHTML = html;
                                            loadMoreEl.style.display = 'none';
                                            
                                            // Reinitialize like buttons in all comments
                                            setTimeout(() => {
                                                const commentLikeButtons = commentsContainer.querySelectorAll('.niriv-like-btn');
                                                commentLikeButtons.forEach(btn => {
                                                    if (!btn.hasAttribute('data-handler-attached')) {
                                                        btn.setAttribute('data-handler-attached', 'true');
                                                        if (typeof nirivLikeSystem !== 'undefined' && nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike) {
                                                            btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                                                e.preventDefault();
                                                                e.stopPropagation();
                                                                nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike(btn);
                                                            });
                                                        }
                                                    }
                                                });
                                                
                                                // Add click handlers for comment like counters to show lightbox likers modal
                                                const commentLikeCounts = commentsContainer.querySelectorAll('.comment-like-wrapper .niriv-like-count');
                                                commentLikeCounts.forEach(countSpan => {
                                                    if (!countSpan.hasAttribute('data-lightbox-handler')) {
                                                        countSpan.setAttribute('data-lightbox-handler', 'true');
                                                        countSpan.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                                                        countSpan.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                                            e.preventDefault();
                                                            e.stopPropagation();
                                                            // Get comment like ID from the like button
                                                            const likeBtn = this.closest('.comment-like-wrapper')?.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn');
                                                            if (likeBtn) {
                                                                const commentLikeId = likeBtn.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                                                                if (commentLikeId) {
                                                                    self.showLightboxLikersModal(commentLikeId, this);
                                                                }
                                                            }
                                                        });
                                                    }
                                                });
                                            }, 100);
                                        };
                                    }
                                }
                            } else {
                                commentsContainer.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #65676b; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">No comments yet</p>';
                                const loadMoreEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-load-more');
                                if (loadMoreEl) loadMoreEl.style.display = 'none';
                            }
                        } else {
                            commentsContainer.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #65676b; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">No comments yet</p>';
                            const loadMoreEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-load-more');
                            if (loadMoreEl) loadMoreEl.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    } else {
                        commentsContainer.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #65676b; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">No comments yet</p>';
                        const loadMoreEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-load-more');
                        if (loadMoreEl) loadMoreEl.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                    
                    // Update comment count
                    if (data.data.count !== undefined) {
                        const commentCountEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comment-count');
                        if (commentCountEl) {
                            const count = data.data.count || 0;
                            if (count > 0) {
                                commentCountEl.textContent = count;
                                commentCountEl.style.display = 'inline';
                            } else {
                                commentCountEl.style.display = 'none';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Reinitialize Lucide icons if available
                    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                        lucide.createIcons();
                    }
                    
                    // Reinitialize like buttons in comments (they're already rendered by PHP)
                    // The universal like system should handle them, but ensure they're initialized
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        const commentLikeButtons = commentsContainer.querySelectorAll('.niriv-like-btn');
                        commentLikeButtons.forEach(btn => {
                            if (!btn.hasAttribute('data-handler-attached')) {
                                btn.setAttribute('data-handler-attached', 'true');
                                if (typeof nirivLikeSystem !== 'undefined' && nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike) {
                                    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                        e.preventDefault();
                                        e.stopPropagation();
                                        nirivLikeSystem.toggleLike(btn);
                                    });
                                }
                            }
                        });
                        
                        // Add click handlers for comment like counters to show lightbox likers modal
                        const commentLikeCounts = commentsContainer.querySelectorAll('.comment-like-wrapper .niriv-like-count');
                        commentLikeCounts.forEach(countSpan => {
                            if (!countSpan.hasAttribute('data-lightbox-handler')) {
                                countSpan.setAttribute('data-lightbox-handler', 'true');
                                countSpan.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                                countSpan.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    e.stopPropagation();
                                    // Get comment like ID from the like button
                                    const likeBtn = this.closest('.comment-like-wrapper')?.querySelector('.niriv-like-btn');
                                    if (likeBtn) {
                                        const commentLikeId = likeBtn.getAttribute('data-post-id');
                                        if (commentLikeId) {
                                            self.showLightboxLikersModal(commentLikeId, this);
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                        });
                    }, 100);
                } else {
                    commentsContainer.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #65676b; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">No comments yet</p>';
                    const loadMoreEl = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-load-more');
                    if (loadMoreEl) loadMoreEl.style.display = 'none';
                }
            })
            .catch(error => {
                console.error('Error loading comments:', error);
                if (commentsContainer) {
                    commentsContainer.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #65676b; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">Error loading comments</p>';
                }
            });
        },
        
        close: function() {
            this.lightbox.classList.remove('active');
            document.body.style.overflow = '';
            this.zoomLevel = 1;
            this.imagePosition = { x: 0, y: 0 };
            this.updateImageTransform();
        },
        
        showImage: function(index) {
            if (index < 0 || index >= this.images.length) return;
            
            this.currentIndex = index;
            const image = this.images[index];
            
            // Reset zoom and position when changing images
            this.zoomLevel = 1;
            this.imagePosition = { x: 0, y: 0 };
            this.updateImageTransform();
            this.updateZoomButtons();
            
            // Update image source
            this.image.src = image.url || image.src;
            this.image.alt = image.caption || image.alt || '';
            
            // Update download link
            document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-download').href = image.url || image.src;
            
            // DO NOT update caption when switching images - keep the post caption
            // The caption is loaded from the post, not from individual images
            
            // IMPORTANT: Preserve post ID - all images are from the same post
            // Don't reload post data when switching images - sidebar data stays the same
            // Only update the image, not the likes/comments/share/author/caption
            // The post ID should remain the same as when lightbox opened
            if (this.originalPostId) {
                this.postId = this.originalPostId;
            }
            
            // DO NOT update caption when switching images - keep the post caption
            // DO NOT reload likes/comments - they're preserved for the post
            
            // Update active thumbnail
            this.updateActiveThumbnail();
            
            // Show/hide navigation buttons
            const prevBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-prev');
            const nextBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-next');
            
            if (this.images.length <= 1) {
                prevBtn.style.display = 'none';
                nextBtn.style.display = 'none';
            } else {
                prevBtn.style.display = index === 0 ? 'none' : 'flex';
                nextBtn.style.display = index === this.images.length - 1 ? 'none' : 'flex';
            }
        },
        
        prev: function() {
            if (this.currentIndex > 0) {
                this.showImage(this.currentIndex - 1);
            }
        },
        
        next: function() {
            if (this.currentIndex < this.images.length - 1) {
                this.showImage(this.currentIndex + 1);
            }
        },
        
        zoomIn: function() {
            if (this.zoomLevel < 10) {
                this.zoomLevel = Math.min(this.zoomLevel + 0.5, 10);
                this.updateImageTransform();
                this.updateZoomButtons();
            }
        },
        
        zoomOut: function() {
            if (this.zoomLevel > 1) {
                this.zoomLevel = Math.max(this.zoomLevel - 0.5, 1);
                if (this.zoomLevel === 1) {
                    this.imagePosition = { x: 0, y: 0 };
                }
                this.updateImageTransform();
                this.updateZoomButtons();
            }
        },
        
        updateImageTransform: function() {
            this.image.style.transform = `translate(${this.imagePosition.x}px, ${this.imagePosition.y}px) scale(${this.zoomLevel})`;
        },
        
        updateZoomButtons: function() {
            const zoomInBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-zoom-in');
            const zoomOutBtn = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-zoom-out');
            
            if (this.zoomLevel > 1) {
                zoomInBtn.style.display = 'none';
                zoomOutBtn.style.display = 'flex';
                this.imageContainer.classList.add('zoomed');
            } else {
                zoomInBtn.style.display = 'flex';
                zoomOutBtn.style.display = 'none';
                this.imageContainer.classList.remove('zoomed');
            }
        },
        
        download: function() {
            const link = document.createElement('a');
            link.href = this.image.src;
            link.download = '';
            link.click();
        },
        
        buildThumbnails: function() {
            const container = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-thumbnails');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            if (this.images.length <= 1) {
                container.style.display = 'none';
                return;
            }
            
            container.style.display = 'flex';
            
            this.images.forEach((img, index) => {
                const thumb = document.createElement('div');
                thumb.className = 'niriv-lightbox-thumbnail';
                if (index === this.currentIndex) {
                    thumb.classList.add('active');
                }
                
                const thumbImg = document.createElement('img');
                thumbImg.src = img.thumbnail || img.url || img.src;
                thumbImg.alt = `Thumbnail ${index + 1}`;
                
                thumb.appendChild(thumbImg);
                
                thumb.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    this.showImage(index);
                });
                
                container.appendChild(thumb);
            });
        },
        
        updateActiveThumbnail: function() {
            const thumbs = document.querySelectorAll('.niriv-lightbox-thumbnail');
            thumbs.forEach((thumb, index) => {
                thumb.classList.toggle('active', index === this.currentIndex);
            });
            
            // Scroll active thumbnail into view
            const activeThumb = thumbs[this.currentIndex];
            if (activeThumb) {
                activeThumb.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest', inline: 'center' });
            }
        },
        
        renderComments: function(comments) {
            const container = document.getElementById('niriv-lightbox-comments');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            if (!comments || comments.length === 0) {
                container.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #65676b; text-align: center; padding: 20px;">No comments yet</p>';
                return;
            }
            
            comments.forEach(comment => {
                const commentEl = document.createElement('div');
                commentEl.className = 'niriv-lightbox-comment';
                
                commentEl.innerHTML = `
                    <img src="${comment.avatar || 'https://www.niriv.com/wp-content/uploads/letter-avatar/4f9814a95b08e0927167f43bad85d53c.svg'}" alt="${comment.author || 'User'}" class="niriv-lightbox-comment-avatar">
                    <div class="niriv-lightbox-comment-content">
                        <div>
                            <span class="niriv-lightbox-comment-author">${comment.author || 'User'}</span>
                            <span class="niriv-lightbox-comment-text">${comment.text || ''}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="niriv-lightbox-comment-actions">
                            <button class="niriv-lightbox-comment-action">Like</button>
                            <button class="niriv-lightbox-comment-action">Reply</button>
                            <span style="color: #65676b; font-size: 12px;">${comment.time || ''}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
                
                container.appendChild(commentEl);
            });
        }
    };
    
    // Initialize when DOM is ready
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => UniversalLightbox.init());
    } else {
        UniversalLightbox.init();
    }
    
    // Expose to global scope
    window.NirivUniversalLightbox = UniversalLightbox;
})();
</script>

<script>
(function() {
    'use strict';
    
    const triggerBtn = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-trigger-btn');
    const overlay = document.getElementById('mobile-menu-overlay');
    const sheet = overlay ? overlay.querySelector('.mobile-menu-sheet') : null;
    
    if (!triggerBtn || !overlay || !sheet) {
        if (window.nirivNotify) {
            window.nirivNotify.log('Mobile menu elements not found', 'warn');
        }
        return;
    }
    
    function openMenu() {
        overlay.hidden = false;
        overlay.removeAttribute('inert');
        triggerBtn.style.display = 'none'; // Hide trigger button
        // Hide go-to-top button when menu is open
        const goToTopBtn = document.getElementById('go-to-top');
        if (goToTopBtn) {
            goToTopBtn.style.display = 'none';
        }
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; // Prevent body scroll
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            overlay.classList.add('is-open');
        });
        
        // Initialize Lucide icons
        if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
            lucide.createIcons();
        }
    }
    
    function closeMenu() {
        overlay.classList.remove('is-open');
        document.body.style.overflow = ''; // Restore body scroll
        setTimeout(() => {
            overlay.hidden = true;
            overlay.setAttribute('inert', '');
            // Restore trigger visibility according to scroll position and viewport
            updateTriggerVisibility();
            // Restore go-to-top button visibility
            const goToTopBtn = document.getElementById('go-to-top');
            if (goToTopBtn && window.pageYOffset > 300) {
                goToTopBtn.style.display = 'flex';
            }
        }, 400);
    }
    
    // Event listeners
    triggerBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        openMenu();
    });
    
    overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target === overlay) {
            closeMenu();
        }
    });
    
    // Close on escape key
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape' && !overlay.hidden) {
            closeMenu();
        }
    });
    
    // Handle create cafe post trigger
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        const triggerLink = e.target.closest('.trigger-create-cafe-post');
        if (triggerLink) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            closeMenu(); // Close the mobile menu first
            
            // Wait a bit for menu to close, then open modal
            setTimeout(function() {
                const modal = document.getElementById('create-post-modal');
                
                // Try multiple methods to open the modal
                if (modal) {
                    // Method 1: Try clicking the open button
                    const openBtn = document.getElementById('open-create-post-modal');
                    if (openBtn) {
                        openBtn.click();
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    // Method 2: Try calling openModal function directly (if in scope)
                    // This will work if the modal script is loaded
                    try {
                        if (typeof window.openModal === 'function') {
                            window.openModal('post');
                            return;
                        }
                    } catch(err) {
                        console.log('openModal not available');
                    }
                    
                    // Method 3: Manually trigger modal display
                    modal.style.display = 'grid';
                    modal.classList.add('is-open');
                    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                    
                    // Initialize icons
                    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                        lucide.createIcons();
                    }
                    
                    // Switch to post tab if tabs exist
                    const postTab = document.querySelector('.cafe-modal-tab[data-tab="post"]');
                    if (postTab) {
                        postTab.click();
                    }
                    return;
                }
                
                // Modal not available on this page, redirect to cafe page
                window.location.href = 'https://www.niriv.com/cafe';
            }, 400);
        }
    });
    
    // Initialize Lucide icons
    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
        lucide.createIcons();
    }
    
    // Re-initialize Lucide icons after AJAX or dynamic content loads
    document.addEventListener('lucide:update', function() {
        if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
            lucide.createIcons();
        }
    });

    // Mobile-only: show the radial trigger button only after scrolling 500px
    const SHOW_THRESHOLD = 500;
    let ticking = false;

    function isRestrictedPage() {
        const body = document.body;
        const classes = body.classList;
        // Restrict: notes, wallet, baje/bazaar, cafe pages
        const restrictedClasses = [
            // Templates
            'page-template-template-notes-php',
            'page-template-template-expense-tracker-php',
            'page-template-template-nfit-php',
            // Common slugs
            'page-notes',
            'page-wallet',
            'page-baje',
            'page-bazaar',
            'page-cafe',
            'page-cafe-create',
            'page-cafe-articles',
            'page-cafe-popular',
            'page-nfit',
            // Cafe single
            'single-cafe_post'
        ];
        for (const cls of restrictedClasses) {
            if (classes.contains(cls)) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    function updateTriggerVisibility() {
        // If menu is open, keep trigger hidden
        if (!overlay.hidden) {
            triggerBtn.style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }
        // Only apply on mobile viewports
        if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
            triggerBtn.style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }
        // Hide on restricted pages
        if (isRestrictedPage()) {
            triggerBtn.style.display = 'none';
            return;
        }
        const scrollY = window.scrollY || window.pageYOffset || 0;
        triggerBtn.style.display = scrollY > SHOW_THRESHOLD ? 'flex' : 'none';
    }

    function onScroll() {
        if (!ticking) {
            requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                updateTriggerVisibility();
                ticking = false;
            });
            ticking = true;
        }
    }

    function onResize() {
        updateTriggerVisibility();
    }

    // Initialize visibility state and listeners
    updateTriggerVisibility();
    window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener('resize', onResize);
})();
</script>

<button id="go-to-top" class="fixed bottom-4 right-6 w-8 h-8 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700 transition-colors rounded-md border border-gray-300 hover:border-gray-400 z-[9998]" aria-label="Go to top" style="display: none; background: #ffffff !important;">
  <i data-lucide="arrow-up" class="w-4 h-4"></i>

<script>
(function() {
  'use strict';
  function initGoToTop() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('go-to-top');
    if (!btn) return;
    function toggle() {
      if (window.pageYOffset > 300) {
        btn.style.display = 'flex';
        btn.style.alignItems = 'center';
        btn.style.justifyContent = 'center';
      } else {
        btn.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' }));
    window.addEventListener('scroll', toggle, { passive: true });
    toggle();
    
    // Initialize Lucide icon for arrow-up
    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
      lucide.createIcons();
    }
  }
  document.readyState === 'loading' ? document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initGoToTop) : initGoToTop();
})();
</script>

<!-- Footer Utility Scripts -->
<script>
(function() {
  'use strict';
  
  // Global error handler for localStorage sandbox errors
  // Suppress errors from external scripts trying to access localStorage in sandboxed iframes
  window.addEventListener('error', function(event) {
    if (event.error && event.error.name === 'SecurityError') {
      const errorMessage = event.error.message || event.message || '';
      if (errorMessage.includes('localStorage') && errorMessage.includes('sandboxed')) {
        // Suppress this error - it's from external scripts in sandboxed iframes
        event.preventDefault();
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }, true);
  
  // Also catch unhandled promise rejections for localStorage errors
  window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', function(event) {
    if (event.reason && event.reason.name === 'SecurityError') {
      const errorMessage = event.reason.message || '';
      if (errorMessage.includes('localStorage') && errorMessage.includes('sandboxed')) {
        // Suppress this error
        event.preventDefault();
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  });
  
  // Font size controls - DISABLED to prevent affecting page content
  // These controls were affecting the entire page font size
  function initFontSizeControls() {
    // Clear any saved font size that might be affecting the page
    if (localStorage.getItem('niriv-font-size')) {
      localStorage.removeItem('niriv-font-size');
      // Reset document font size to default
      document.documentElement.style.fontSize = '';
    }
    
    const decreaseBtn = document.getElementById('font-decrease');
    const increaseBtn = document.getElementById('font-increase');
    
    if (!decreaseBtn || !increaseBtn) return;
    
    // Disable font size controls to prevent affecting page content
    decreaseBtn.style.opacity = '0.5';
    decreaseBtn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
    increaseBtn.style.opacity = '0.5';
    increaseBtn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
    
    // Remove event listeners by replacing with no-op
    decreaseBtn.onclick = function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      return false;
    };
    increaseBtn.onclick = function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      return false;
    };
  }
  
  // Initialize all
  function init() {
    initFontSizeControls();
    
    // Initialize Lucide icons
    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
      lucide.createIcons();
    }
  }
  
  document.readyState === 'loading' ? 
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init) : 
    init();
})();
</script>

<script>
(function() {
  'use strict';
  function initScrollProgress() {
    const bar = document.getElementById('scroll-progress-bar');
    if (!bar) return;
    function update() {
      const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
      const height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
      bar.style.width = (scrollTop / height) * 100 + '%';
    }
    window.addEventListener('scroll', update, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener('resize', update);
    update();
  }
  document.readyState === 'loading' ? document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initScrollProgress) : initScrollProgress();
})();

// Mobile Footer Visibility Behavior - Hide only when in footer area
(function() {
  let footer = null;
  let ticking = false;

  function initMobileFooterBehavior() {
    // Only apply on mobile devices
    if (window.innerWidth > 768) return;
    
    // Look for mobile navigation footer (sticky bottom nav)
    footer = document.querySelector('#mobile-footer-menu');
    
    if (!footer) return;

    // Keep footer always visible
    footer.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
    footer.style.transition = 'transform 0.3s ease-in-out';
    footer.style.opacity = '1';

    function handleScroll() {
      if (!ticking) {
        requestAnimationFrame(updateFooterVisibility);
        ticking = true;
      }
    }

    function updateFooterVisibility() {
      const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
      const documentHeight = document.documentElement.scrollHeight;
      const windowHeight = window.innerHeight;
      const footerElement = document.querySelector('footer');
      
      // Hide footer menu only when scrolled into the footer area
      if (footerElement) {
        const footerTop = footerElement.offsetTop;
        const isInFooterArea = scrollTop + windowHeight >= footerTop - 100; // 100px buffer
        
        if (isInFooterArea) {
          footer.style.transform = 'translateY(100%)';
          footer.style.opacity = '0';
        } else {
          footer.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
          footer.style.opacity = '1';
        }
      }
      
      ticking = false;
    }

    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll, { passive: true });
    
    // Reset on window resize
    window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
      if (window.innerWidth > 768 && footer) {
        // Reset footer styles on desktop
        footer.style.transform = '';
        footer.style.transition = '';
        footer.style.opacity = '';
      } else if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
        // Re-initialize on mobile
        initMobileFooterBehavior();
      }
    });
  }

  // Initialize on page load
  document.readyState === 'loading' ? 
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initMobileFooterBehavior) : 
    initMobileFooterBehavior();
})();
</script>

</body>
